SUDHA_1.ACIHsatyam.h | na brahmasvarUpanirUpaNe kimapyavashiShyam.h | tathA.api tattu samanvayadityupakramAditAtparyaliN^gabalAtsakalasyApi shAstrasya yo brahmaNi paramamukhyayA vR^ittyA pratipAdyapratipAdakatvalakShaNasamanvayo.abhihitastameva samanvayaM vibhAgena prapaJNchenAnandamaya ityAdinA.adhyAyena vadati sUtrakAra iti na vaiyarthyam.h | tattu samanvayAditi hi pratij~nAmAtreNokttam.h | tadyAvadudAharaNatvena vAkyavisheShAnupAdAya vimarshapUrvakaM pUrvottarapakShopAlambhasAdhanAbhyAM na prapaJNchyate tAvadanukttaprAyamarkAkAritvAt.h | anyathA paro.api hyanyadeva samanvayAdityuktavA kR^itI syAt.h | yadi hi pratyayamanutpAdyaiko.ayaM bhUmadhyapradesha iti brUyAt.h | tadA paro.api kiM na brUyAtparastAdvitasteriti | tasmAdAvashyakaM samanvayaprapaJNchanam.h | tadanena samanvayasUtreNAdhyAyasheShasya prapaJNchyaprapaJNchakabhAvena saN^gatirdarshitA | evaM tarhi tadAnantaryameva syAtkutovyavadhAnamityata ukttamevamiti | evamIkShatyadhikaraNavyutpAditanyAyena brahmaNaH shAstrAvagamyatve mukhyayA vR^ittyA sakalashAstrapratipAdyatve sambhAvite satIti | etadukttaM bhavati | satyaM prapaJNchanamanantaraprAptam.h tathA.apyavAchyatvAdyAshaN^kAnirAsena shAstrAvagamyatvasambhAvanAsamarthanena vyavadhIyate | sati hi tasminna(nneta)syAvasaraH | shabdaleshasaJNchArAsambhave vAkyatAtparyavichArasyAnavakAshatvAt.h | nahi toyAbhyavahArAsamarthasya mumUrShoH shaShkulIbhakShaNaM sachetanaH sambhAvayatIti | "svAdiShvasarvanAmasthAne' iti padasaMj~nA.anushAsanAdatra na yatibhaN^gashshaN^kanIyaH | 
SUDHA_1.ACIHtadidamanupapannam.h | brahmaNo dvairUpyasyAprAmANikatvAt.h | sarvANyapi hi vedavAkyAnyasaN^khayeyakalyANaguNAkaraM sakaladoShagandhavidhuramekarUpameva brahma nArAyaNAkhyaM pratipAdayanti | kintu kAnichitsarvaj~natvasarveshvaratvasavarAntaryAmitvasaundaryaudAryavIryAdiguNavishiShyatayA | kAnichidapahatapApmatvanirduHkhatvaprAkR^itabhautikavigraharahitatvAdidoShAbhAvavishiShyatayA |  kAnichitadigahanatAj~nApanAya vAN^manasAgocharatvAdyAkAreNa | kAnichitsarvaparihAreNa tasyaivopAdAnAyAdvitIyatvena | kAnichitsarvasattApratItipravR^ittinimittatApratipattyarthaM sarvAtmakatvena ityevamAdyanekaprakAraiH paramapuruShaM bodhayanti | tato vyAkulabuddhayo gurusampradAyavikalA ashrutavedavyAkhyAtAraH sarvatrApyekarUpatAmananusandadhAnA vedaM Chindanti | na (cha)etad.hdvairUpyaprapaJNchanamuttaratropalabhyate | nApyasyAvidyAviShayasya prapaJNchanaM mokShashAstre.atropayujyate | prasaN^gAduchyata iti chenna | sarvasva prAsaN^gikatve pratipAdyAbhAvaprasaN^gAt.h | tadidamAbhANakaM laukikAnAM nAtivartate "sArthAdapi taskarA bahavaH' iti | etachcha saguNanirguNabhedaM nirAkurvatA.a.achAryeNa nirastamiti neha punaH prakrAntam.h | tathAcha bhAShyam.h | nAnyathA tadadR^iShyeriti | 
SUDHA_1.ACIHtaittirIyake sa vA eSha puruSho.annarasamaya ityadinA.annamayaprANamayamanomayavij~nAnamayAnandamayAH paThyante | tatra saMshayaH | kimete.annamayAdayaH paramAtmaiva | uta tadanyaH kashchiditi | sarvatra brahmashabdashravaNAttasya cha viShNAvanyatra cha prayogAt.h | kiM tAvatprAptam.h | anya evAnnamayAdishabdArtha iti | kutaH | annamayAdishabdA hi vikaravAchinaH | mayaT.h pratyayasya vikArAthare.anushAsanAt.h | vikArasya cha sharIrAdikosheShu sambhavAt.h | sarvavikArAtmakatvena prakR^itau vopapatteH | jIvAnAM vA vikArAbhimAninAmannamayatvAdikaM yukttam.h | gauraH shyAma ityAdivat.h | adhiShThAtrINAM brahmAdidevatAnAM vA.ayaM shabdaH sambhavati | ashanirindra itivat.h | nacha vikAratvaM parasya brahmaNaH sambhavati | nirvikAro.akSharaH shuddha ityAdeH | yadyapi vikAra iva prAchurye.api mayaT.hpratyayo.asti | tathA.apyannamayashabdastAvadvikArArtho.aN^gIkAryaH | "oShadhIbhyo.annamannAtpuruShaH' ityoShadhijanitAnnavikAraM puruShashabdAbhidheyaM sharIraM prakR^itya "sa vA eSha puruSho.annamannarasamayaH' ityukttatvAt.h | "tasyedameva shiraH' ityaparokShatayA nirdeshAt.h | tathAcha dvaividhyakalpanA.anupapatteH sarvatra vikArArtha evAN^gIkAryaH | kiJNchAnnamayAdayaH paJNcha, brahma tvekameva, ataH kathaM tadetaiH shabdairuchyeta | api chaite parasparamanyatayA sharIrasharIribhAvenAntaratvena chochyante | nachaivaM brahma bhavitumarhati | nacha tarhyAnandamayo.astu brahma sarvAntaratvAditi vAchyam.h | vikArapravAhapatitatvAt.h | annamayAdyAntaratvamAtreNa sarvAntaratvAnishchayAt.h | kiJNcha brahmavidApnoti paramiti prakR^itaM paraM brahma Anandamayasya "brahma puchChaM pratiShThA' ityavayavatayA pratIyate | nachAvayava evAvayavI, virodhAt.h | ato na annamayAdayaH paJNchApi brahma kiM tvanya eveti | evaM prApte siddhAntayatsUtraM vyAkhyAti- samudrashAyinamiti || 
SUDHA_1.ACIHatra taittirIyake "anyAsu chatadUShAsu shAkhAsvapi sahasrashaH | Anandamaya ityAdyaiH shabdairvAchyo hariH svayam.h' ityetAvatA.a.anandamayo brahmeti pratij~nAbhAgo vyAkhyAtaH | tatra taittirIyaka ityudAharaNavAkyagrahaNam.h | anyAsviti nirNetavyavyapadeshaH | etadrUpAsviti guNisAmAnyaguNavAchinAmavatIShvityarthaH | tatra heturabhyAsAditi | tadvayAkhyAnaM ye.annamiti | "ye.annaM brahmopAsate, ye prANaM brahmopAsate, AnandaM brahmaNo vidvAn.h, vij~nAnaM brahma chedveda, asadbrahmeti veda chet.h' ityannamayAdiviShayatayodAhR^iteShu shlokeShu brahmashabdasyAbhyAsAdityarthaH | ekaviShayAsakR^idukttirmukhyo.abhyAsaH | na chaivamatrAsti | kiM tvasakR^idakttimAtra(mitij~nApa)miti shaN^kAyAmekaviShayatA.apyastIti j~nApayitumityAderityanuktavA ityAdirUpAdityukttam.h | annamayAdiviShayatvena brahmashabdasya shrutatvAdityukttaM bhavati | brahmashabdena kathamayaM nishchaya ityata Aha- brahmashabdasyeti || tadapi kuta ityata Aha- shrutiriti || "tadeva brahma paramam.h' iti sAvadhR^itiH shrutiH viShNumeva brahmashabdavAchyaM jagau yato.ata iti yojanA | tatrApi taditi parAmarshaviShayo viShNuriti kuta ityata ukttam.h- samudrashAyinamiti || vyAkhyAtametatprathamasUtre | 
SUDHA_1.ACIHannamayAdInAmabrahmatve vikArashabdaH sAdhAraNopapattiH | AnandamayarUpe tu brahmavidApnoti paramityukttasya "brahma puchChaM pratiShThA' iti puchChatvoktayA samastasyAvayavina AnandamayasyAbrahmatvaprAptiradhikA.apyupapattirastItyato.atrAviIhatairbhavitavyamiti j~nApayitumAnandamayanAma gR^ihItaM sUtrakR^itetyanyathopapattirukttA bhava(tI)ti | yadyAnandamayo brahma syAttadA tadavayavasya samastAyA mukhyAyA AbrahmatAyAH samyagbrahmatAyA aprApteriti vA | tatashcha tadvedanAtparaprAptiH shrutA bAdhyeteti | nanvannamaye.apyadhikA.anupapattirasti | "oShadhIbhyo.annam.h | annAtpuruShaH | sa vA eSha puuruSho.annarasamayaH' iti | "tasyedameva shiraH' iti cha | maivam.h | asyApi vikAropapAdakatvena tadantarbhAvAt.h | yadvA athAto brahmajij~nAseti jij~nAsyatayokttasya brahmaNaH puchChatvoktayA samastAbrahmatAprApterAnandamayavichArasya prakR^itena saN^gatatvAdAnandamayanAmagrahaNamiti yojyam.h | 
SUDHA_1.ACIHdvitIye vyAptyabhAvaM darshayati- yathaiveti || etachcha "udbabarhAtmanaH keshau' ityAdinA purANe prasiddham.h | akhilA nirupacharitA | tathA.a.anandamayAvayavasyApi bhaviShyatIti sheShaH | atra pramANamAha- darshitA cheti || pArthadarshanaM cha dyAvApR^ithivyorityAdi tadvAkyAdavagamyate | chashabdaH purANAdyukttisamuchchayArthaH | evashabdastvevaM pramitaiva na vAN^mAtreNochyata iti sambaddhayate | nanu loke yo.avayavaH sa parichChinno dR^iShyastatkathametadityataH parameshvarasyAghaTitaghaTakatayA sarvatrApratibaddhayA shaktayA.anyatrAdR^iShyamapi ghaTate kA.atra kathantetyAha- niHsImA iti || sImasIme striyAmubhe iti sIman.h shabdaparyAyasImAshabdottarapado.ayaM samAsaH | sImanshabdottarapadatve.api DAbubhAbhyAmanyatarasyAmiti sAdhu |

SUDHA_1.ACIHchashabdo.avadhAraNe | atra shrutau | kuta ityata Aha- pratipAditA iti || ayamarthaH | mayaT.hshabdo hi vikAra iva prAchurye.api mukhyaH | tatprakR^itavachane mayaDityanushAsanAt.h | nacha brahmashabdo.anyatra mukhyaH | nacha sAvakAshena niravakAshasya bAdho.asti | ato niravakAshabrahmashabdabalAtsAvakAshasya mayaTaH prAchuryArthatvopapatterna tadbalAdannamayAdInAmaparamAtmatvaM kalpyamiti | etena vikArapravAhamadhyapatitatvAnnAnandamayashabdaH prAchuryArtha ityetadgarbhasrAveNaiva gatam.h | annamayAdiShvapi mayaTaH prAchuyarArthatAsvIkArAt.h | pareNApi hi prANamaye na vikArArthatvaM vakttuM yukttam.h | prANAnAM prANavikAratvAsambhavAt.h | yathAkathaJNchidvikArakalpane mukhyArthaparityAgAt.h | syAdetat.h | annavikAratvavadannaprAchuryamapi neshvarasya sambhavati | taddhi pAthirvasharIrANAmannopajIvinAM syAditi chenna | atrAnnashabdasya prasiddhAnnArthatvAbhAvAt.h | svayameva hi shrutiH "adyate.atti cha bhUtAni tasmAdannaM taduchyate' ityannashabdaM nirvaktti | adidhAtoH karmaNi kartari cha kttapratyaye sati rUpametat.h | nacha bhUtAttR^itvaM prasiddhAnnasya sambhavati | tasmAdannashabdo.ayaM bhAvapradhAno bhUtAdyatvaM bhUtAttR^itvaM cha vaktti |

SUDHA_2.ACIHyadyapi sa prabhurviShNurdUrato.api tattachChakttiprabodhane.atishakttastathA.api kevalaM lIlayA tatratatra sthitastattattachChakttInAM prabodhako bhavatIti j~nApayituM sarvagatatvamiha pravichAryata iti sambandhaH | etadukttaM bhavati | svanirgamapraveshAbhyAM dehapAtanotthApanamityAdyA mukhyaprANAdishakttayastadantargatabhagavadAyattA iti prAgukttam.h | tadanupapannam.h | bhagavataH sarvagatatvAbhAvAt.h | shAstraikasamadhigamyaM khalu (hi) tat.h | shAstraM chaitamasyAmityAdikamanyaparamityAshaN^kayokttArthasamarthanAya sarvagatatvamatra harerupapadyata iti | athavA na sarvagatatvaM harerupapAdanIyam.h | tasyAnandAdivatsraShyR^itvAdivadvA guNatvAbhAvAdityAshaN^kaya na savargatatvaM nAma sarvasaMyogitvamAtramiha vivakShitam.h | kiM nAma tattachChakttiprerakatvena | atastadupapAdanamupapadyata ityanenochyate | athavA na sarvagatatvamatra pratipAdanIyam.h | adR^ishyatvAdyadhikaraNe tasya pratipAdayiShyamANatvAdityAshaN^kaya tatra savargatatvamAtramatra tu tattachChakttiprabodhakatvamiti tAtparyabhedo.anenochyate | athavA antaryAmyadhikaraNe pR^ithivyAdiShu sthitevarkShyamANatvAnnedamArambhaNIyamityAshaN^kayAtra shakttiprerakatvena tatra tu sattAdipradatvena tattadantargatatvamuchyata ityanenAchaShye | athavA antaHsthatvAdhikaraNenedaM gatArthamityAshaN^kaya tatra chandrAdikatipayapadArthAntarasthitatvam.h atra tu sarvapadArthAntargatatvamabhidhIyata iti pratipAdyabhedametenAha | athavA | sarvagatatvaM nAma sarvamUrta(dravyasaMyogitvaM vA) paramamahatparimANayogitvaM vA (su)prasiddham.h | tadatra yadi sAdhyaM syAttadA.arbhakaukastvAdityAkShepAnupapattiradR^ishyatvAdyadhikaraNena gatArthatA echetyAshaN^kaya sarvagatatvamanyathA.anena vyAchaShye |

SUDHA_2.ACIHkiJNcha dvitantukArambhake(vayave)tantau karmotpannaM tantvantarAdvibhAgaM karoti | tato dvitantukArambhakasaMyogavinAshaH | tannAshe dvitantukavinAshaH | athedAnIM tantoH kAryasaMyukttapradeshavibhAgaH | tatashchottaradeshasaMyogaH | tasmAtkarmaNo vinAsha iti pareShAM prakriyA | evaM cha yathA.anekakAlavartinyapi kriyA kadAchitsaMyogAdyArabhate na yAvatsattvam.h | tathA nityApi kadAchitsaMyogAdyArabhatAM ko virodhaH | sAmAnyavattve satyasmadAdibAhyendriyagrAhyatvaM heturastviti chenna | visheShyAsiddheH | bAhyendriyagrAhyasajAtIyatvasya paramANvAdau vyabhichArAt.h | kiJNcha varNanityatve sphuTo.asya vyabhichAraH | nApyAgamAdIshvarakriyA.anityatAvagatiH | sa hIshvarakriyA.anityetyevamAtmako vA, sa imAnlokAnasR^ijatetyevamAtmako vA | Adyastu nopalabhyate | dvitIyastu sa aikShata so.akAmayatetyAdinA tulyaH | tatra yadi kriyAyA anityatvaM, j~nAnAderapi kuto na bhavediti | astu tarhi nityatve bAdhakasadbhAvAditi dvitIyaH pakShaH | tathA hi | yadi sR^iShyisamaye.api saMhArakriyA vidyeta tadA tathaiva shrutyAdAvupalabhyeta | jananavinAshau cha ghaTasya yugapatprasajyeyAtAm.h | kiJNcha yadIshvarakriyA nityA syAttarhi kriyAyAH saMyogavibhAgau prati anapekShakAraNatvAttadutpattisAtatyaprasaN^gaH | api cheshvarakriyA saMyogavibhAgau karoti na vA | neti pakShe kriyAtvaM vyAhanyeta | Adye.api kiM svasattottarakShaNe uta viramya | nAdyaH | svasattAyA idaM prathamatAbhAvena saMyogAdivisheShasya vivakShitakShaNAdapi pUrvamutpattiprasaN^gAt.h | na dvitIyaH | pUrvottarAvasthayoravishiShyasya viramyavyApArAyogAt.h | uttarasaMyogasya karmavinAshakatvena kR^itasaMyogasya karmaNo.avasthAnAnupapatteshchetyata ukttaM shaktayAtmaneti | ayamarthaH | tattatkAryajananashakttireva kriyetyuchyate | ataH tena rUpeNa sthirA sA yadA vyajyate tadA vyavahArAlambanaM tattatkAryajananI cha bhavatIti na kashchiddoSha iti | kriyA shaktayAtmanA vyakttishakttirUpeNa kAraNeneti vA |

SUDHA_3.ACIHyoga iti yogavR^ittiviShayaH parameshvaraH | rUDhaH prasiddhaH prakR^ityAdiH | ayamarthaH | asti tAvadviditapadapadArthasaN^gateradhigatashAbdanyAyasyAjAdishabdashravaNe brahmaNa iva pradhAnasyApi buddhAvArohaH, dhiyAM cha (tu) svata eva prAmANyam.h | aprAmANyaM tu bAdhakAdhInamityupapAditaM prathamasUtre | nachAtrArthadvayayAbhyupagame bAdhakamasti | yena buddhAvArUDhamapi tyajyeta | ato nirapavAdapratItibalAtsarveShAmapi shabdAnAmubhayArthatvameShyavyamiti |
SUDHA_3.ACIHatra kashchit.h andhAnugatAndha iva prakR^itishchetyAdIni sUtrANi brahmaNo jagadupAdAnatApratipAdakatayA vyAkhyAyoktadUShaNagaNAdbhItaH sUtratAtparyamAha ""paramasUkShmAchidrUpapradhAnasharIraM brahma "yo.avyakte tiShThanyasyAvyaktaM sharIram.h' ityAdishrutisiddham.h | tathAcha brahmAdhiShThitaM brahmAtmakaM pradhAnaM jagadupAdAnamiti brahmaiva jagadupAdAnatayA(.aN^gIkri)gIyate | ato noktadoShaH'' iti | taM pratyAha- upAdAnatvameveti ||
SUDHA_3.ACIHetaduktaM bhavati | pitrAdidR^iShyAntAnAmayaM khalu niShkR^iShyo.arthaH | yatpitrAdyupabhuktamannaM tachCharIrI(ra)bhUtaM putrAdigatAchetanAMshopAdAnaM bhavatIti | pakShAntarasyAsambhAvitatvAt.h | nachAyamasmAkamaniShyaH | mahApralaye parameshvareNa nigIrNaM mahadAdikAyarM tachCharIrarUpakapradhAnatAM gachChati | tachcha pradhAnaM punarmahadAdikAyaropAdAnaM bhavatItyaN^gIkArAditi | etenorNanAbhyAdInAM na vikAritvaM(tA)chennirupAdAnA tantvAdyutpattiH prasajyata ityapi nirastam.h | 
SUDHA_3.ACIHathavA mahadAdikaM na chetanavikAraH, achetanatvAdghaTavaditi yuktyantaraviruddhaM cha brahmaNo jagadupAdAnatvamiti chetasi nidhAyAsya vyAptimupapAdayati- na chetaneti || nanu ghaTAdayo.api brahmavikArA iti chenna | mR^idAdivikAratvasya pramitatvAt.h | paramparayeti chet.h | evaM tarhi na svayaM chetanavikArAH | kintu tatkAraNAnItyuktaM syAt.h | tathAcha kathaM na dR^iShyAntatA | tarhi tatkAraNeShu vyabhichAra iti chenna | teShAmeva pakShatvAt.h | sukhaduHkhAdiShvanaikAntikatvamiti chenna | teShAmantaHkaraNavikAratvAbhyupagamAt.h | etenaitadapi pratyuktam.h | jagat.h, abhinnanimittopAdAnam.h prekShApUrvajanitakAryatvAtsukhAdivaditi | ghaTAdiShu vyabhichAra(rAchcha)shcha | teShAmapi pakShIkaraNe pramANabAdhaH syAt.h | nanvachetanamapi jagachchetanavikArashchettadA ko doShaH syAt.h | evaM tarhi chetano.apyachetanavikAraH syAt.h H na chaitadastItyAha- nAchetaneti ||
SUDHA_3.ACIHparasparamatyantAbhinne dve vastunI | tatraikaM nirvikAraM jagannimittameva | aparaM tu pariNAmi jagadupAdAnatamevetyaN^gIkAre neshvarasya kevalanimittatvavAdinAmasmAkaM kashchidvivAdaH | nirvikArasya jagannimittasyAsmAbhirIshvaratvena, pariNAmino jagadupAdAnasya pradhAnatvena svIkR^itatvAt.h | vivAdAbhAvAchcha prakR^itishcheti(tyAdi)sUtrANAmanArambha eveti | atra yo bhAga iti parAbhyupagamenoktam.h | svamatena tu yadvastviti j~nAtavyam.h | nahi bhAgina vinA bhAgaH sambhavati | nApi vikAryavikAriNoH kashchidbhAgI vidyate | 
SUDHA_3.ACIHjagadbhAvaM vinA sattvAdidharmayogena brahmaiva tathA sattyadAdikamuchyate | tarhi tadanupravishyetyasyAnvayo nAsti | nahi brahmaNaH sattvAdidharmayoge sadAdishabdavAchyatve vA jagatpraveshasyopayogo.asti | nApi tataH pUrvakAlInatA | kiJNchaivaM sati prasiddhivirodhaH sattyadAdishabdAnAM "dve vA va brahmaNo rUpe' ityAdau mUrtAmUrtavAchitayA prasiddhatvAt.h ityato jagadgatena rUpeNetyuktam.h | yadyapyananyApekShayA sarvadA sattvAdidharmayogaH sadAdishabdavAchyatA cha brahmaNaH | tathA.api tattadvastugatarUpeNaiva tattachChabdavAchyatvamityasti vyavasthA | tathAcha mUrtAmUrtajagadgatena rUpeNa brahmasadAdishabdavAchyamityataH tadanupravishyeti sambaddhayate | parameshvarasannidhAnAdeva mUrtAmUrtAderapi sadAdishabdavAchyatA chopapadyata iti |
SUDHA_3.ACIHbhavatItyaniruktam.h | tathA.api niruktamityanena virodhAtsamyak.h kAtsnaryena vaktumashakyatvata ityuktam.h | nanu vedetarapramANenAniruktamiti kuto na vyAkhyAyate | na | prakR^itaparityAgaprasaN^gAt.h | vedena niruktamiti (hi) prakR^itam.h | kiJNchokteH shabdadharmatvAtpratyakShAnumAnAbhyAmaniruktamityayuktam.h | smR^itInAmapi vedAtmakatvena virodhatAdavasthyam.h | mahimAdhikyaM chAtra labhyata iti | jagadAshrayatvAnnilayanam.h | nishchitamayante pravartante.asminniti | ro la iti yogavibhAgAllatvam.h | nipUrvasya lI(N^.h)shleShaNa ityasya vA.adhikaraNe lyuTi kR^ite rUpametat.h | svAshrayatvAdanilayanam.h | na vidyate svAtiriktaM nilayanaM yasyeti | j~nAnatvAdvisheShaj~nAnarUpatvAdvij~nAnam.h | durvidatvato durj~neyatvAdavij~nAnam.h | na vidyate vij~nAnaM sakalavisheShAvagAhijIvaj~nAnaM yadviShaya iti | sattateH samyagvyApteryAtAnAdyatanaM prati hetutvAchcha satyam.h | tanoteH D.hvipratyaye takAramAtraM rUpam.h | tena sachChabdasya bahuvrIhiH | yatI prayatna ityasyAntarNItaNyarthasya Dapratyaye (yamiti) rUpam.h | tataH karmadhArayaH | "ayasmAyadIni Chandasi' iti bhasaMj~nAshrayaNAjjashtvAbhAvaH | durjanairaprApyatvAdevAnR^itaJNcha | natu mithyAtvAt.h | yadyapi R^itaM prAptaM netyanR^itam.h | tathA.api "brahmavidApnoti param.h' ityAdishrutivirodhaparihArAya durjanairityuktam.h | hishabdo brahmaNo mithyAtvAbhAve prasiddhiM dyotayati | nityasAdhuguNavyAptiyantR^irUpatvataH satyam.h | atra nityatvata ityekaM vyAkhyAnam.h | nityasatyashabdayoraikAthyarsya vakShyamANatvAt.h | sat.h sAdhuguNAH "sadbhAve sAdhubhAve cha' iti | vachanAt.h teShAM vyAptirbAhulyaM takAreNoktam.h | pUrvavattanoterbhAve D.hvipratyayaH | tasya yantR^irUpatvAdyam.h | yama uparama iti dhAtoH (ityato) DaH | bhakteShu sAdhuguNabAhulyaprerakatvAditi yAvat.h | abhavaditi vachanAdbrahmaNaH sattvAdikaM sAdIti shaN^kAnirAsAyoktam.h- sadeti || pratyekaM chAsya sambandhaH | 
SUDHA_3.ACIHtathAhi | kiM brahmaNaH svata eva vishvAkArapariNAmaH | kiM vA parataH | nAdyaH, kvApyadarshanAt.h | yadapi kShIravaddhItyudAhR^itam.h | tat.h kAlAdervidyamAnatvAdayuktam.h | svechChayaiveti chenna | prayojanAbhAvAt.h | svabhAvo.ayamiti chenna | prekShAvattvahAneH | na dvitIyaH | advitIyatvAt.h | nacha niravayavaM kvApi pariNataM dR^iShyam.h | AkAshaM saMyogAdimadupalabdhamiti chenna | dravyAkAraNapariNAmasya prakR^itatvAt.h | paramANvAdayastu svarUpeNaiva na siddhA iti | 
SUDHA_3.ACIHsatyakAraNaguNapUrvakatvAt.h, ayAvad.hdravyabhAvitvAt.h | sukhAdivat.h | sparshava(dvisheShaguNa)tve tadanupalambhaprasaN^gaH | shabdo hi shrotreNa prApto vA gR^ihyate.aprApto vA | aprAptagrahaNe.atiprasaN^gaH | prAptistu shabdashravasorna sambhavati | sA hi na tAvachChrotrasya gamanena sambhavati | tasyAmUtarsya gatyabhA(terasambha)vAt.h | nApi shabdasyAgamanena | sa hi na tAvachChaN^khAdikamAshrayaM parityajyAgantumalam.h | guNatvAt.h | nApi shaN^khAdyAgamanena shrotra(sya)pratyAsattiH | tadanupalambhAt.h | nacha shabdAntarotpAdaparamparayA | guNasya svAshraye svAshrayAshrite vA guNe.asamavAyikAraNatvAt.h | nacha shaN^khashravasormadhye shaN^kho vA tadArabdhadravyaM vA.asti | tasmAchChaN^khAdinimittAnyapahAyAshrayAntare vartamAno vIchItaraN^ganyAyena karNashaShkulI(ga)mantamAkAshadeshamApanna upalabhyate nAnyatheti sthitam.h | nApyAtmaguNaH | bAhyendriyapratyakShatvAdAtmAntaragrAhyatvAdAtmanyasamavAyAt.h ahaN^kAreNa vibhaktasya grahaNAdUpAdivat.h | na vikkAlamanasAM (guNaH), pratyakShatvAdvisheShaguNatvAchcha' iti prasaktapratiShedhe parisheShAdebhyo.atiriktaM dravyaM siddhayati | tadAkAshamiti |
SUDHA_3.ACIHdvitIye tvAshrayadravyasiddhAvapi nAkAshasiddhiH | pR^ithivyAdiguNatvopapatteH | pratyakShatve satyakAraNaguNapUrvakatvAyAvad.hdravyabhAvitvayoH piTharapAkapakShe tadgatarUpAdinA vyabhichArAt.h | pratyakShatve satIti cha kimarthaM vaktavyam.h | pArthivaparamANurUpAdi(vyAvR^ittya)parihArArthamiti chet.h, kutastatpariharaNIyam.h | pramitatvAditi chet.h | tarhi shabdasyApi shaN^khAdyAshrayatayA pramitatvAdvayAptigrahaNasamaye tadvayavachChedAtharM (api) visheShaNamupAdeyameva | nacha sparshavadvisheShaguNatve bAdhakaM pashyAmaH | anupalabdhistu na prasajyate | chakShuSha iva shrotrasya gatyA sannikarShopapatteH | amUrtasya tadanupapattistu AkAshasiddhayuttarakAlInaiva | shrotrasya chakShuSha iva gatvAgrAhitve shabde diksaMshayo na syAditi chet.h | agatvAgrAhitve diN^.hnishchayo.api na syAt.h | saMshayAdapi nishchayo mahIyAn.h (garIyAn.h) | shaN^khAdyavayavAgamanena vA sannikarShopapattiH | na choktadoShaH | ghrANagandhasannikarShatulyayogakShematvAt.h |

SUDHA_3.ACIHatha balIpalitakArkashyAdinA kAlasambandhe.anumite, vipratipannaM prati parAparAdipratyayAnAM kAryatvena nimittAnumAnamidaM bhAShyamiti | maivam.h | sharIrAvasthayA hi tasya kAlasambandho.anumIyate, yatkiJNchid.hdravyasambandho vA | Adye kimasmAdanumAnAtprAkkAlaH siddho.athavA neti vAchyam.h | Adye tannityasiddhestasya kAlasya prAganumAnAnnityena sAkShiNA siddheH | dvitIye chAprasiddhavisheShaNatvAnnAnumAnAvasaro bhavet.h | kiJNcha valIpalitA(kArkashya)disharIrAvasthA kAraNatvena kAlAnumAne tannityasiddhestasya kAlasambandhasya nityaM sarvadA valIpalitAdivaidhuryadashAyAmapi siddhernitye paramANAvapi siddherbAdhitaviShayatvena nAnumAnAvasaro bhavet.h |

SUDHA_3.ACIHanyathetyAdyanyathA vyAkhyAyate | anyathA sAkShiNaH prapaJNchagrAhakapratyakShAdyAtyantikaprAmANyAgrAhakatve, vishvasya viyadAderuttarakShaNa eva nivR^ittirvinAshaH kiM na shaN^kayate | tathAcha sarvapravR^ittivilayaH syAt.h | parameshvarasaJNjihIrShAdyabhAvAdityata uktam.h- akasmAditi || (anu-1117 pR^iShThe draShyavyam.h |) nanvIshvarechChayaiva shrutismR^itItihAsapurANAni prapaJNchapralayaM pratipAdayanti, vishvavinAsho na nirhetuko vinAshatvAtpaTanAshavadityanumAnamapi | tatkathamevaM shaN^kayata ityata uktam.h- shrutIti || pramANAnAM nivR^ittirnAmAtyantikaprAmANyAbhAvaH | tAtparyaM pUvarvat.h | 
SUDHA_3.ACIHathavA no saMsR^itergatirityuktam.h | saMsAragateH shrutyAdisiddhatvAt.h | tadasiddhayA cha hetorvisheShaNAdityata Aha- vAkyeti || brahmaNo.api nivR^ittyAshaN^kAyAmApAditAyAM yadi paro vAkyAnumAdito nivR^ittyabhAvanishchayaH syAditi brUyAt.h, yadi vA AkasmikottarakShaNe pralayashaN^kApAdane vAkyAnumAditaH parameshvarechChAdinaiva syAditi manyeta, yadi cha vAkyAnumAditaH saMsAranivR^ittiH syAditi vadet.h, tadA tasya vAkyAdeH prAmANyaM kena nishchitamiti vaktavyam.h | sAkShItareNetyaN^gIkAre j~nAnasya sAkShivedyatvena parataH prAmANyagrahApatteH sAkShiNaiveti vaktavyam.h | 
SUDHA_3.ACIHyaH parasya prativAdyAdeH satyatAM jAnannapi paro nAstIti vadati | sa svAtmataskara iti yojanA | svAtmAnamiva paramapi satyatayA pashyato.ahameka eva satyo madaj~nAnakalpitAH sarve jIvA jaDAshcheti vachanaM svAnubhavaviruddhamityarthaH | nahi tvadaj~nAnaparikalpitaM samastamityatra balavatpramANamasti | yena darshanamapi bAdhyeta | nahi sattvena pratIyamAnasyApi gandharvanagarAderasattvamevAN^gIkriyate | kintu balavatpramANabAdhAt.h | anyathA prativAdyaj~nAnakalpitastvamiti kathaM na syAH | tathA chAnishchayena na mokShArthA pravR^ittiH syAditi |

SUDHA_3.ACIHnanvatra sUtragR^ihItatayA pareNopAttAnAM shrutInAmanupapattyAdikaM prathamatA vaktavyam.h | satyam.h | tathA.apyekajIvAj~nAnaparikalpitatve samastasya, na pramANamastItyanantaramevoktam.h | asyAM cha tadApAtataH pratIyate | "anAdimAyayA supto yadA jIvaH prabuddhayate' ityuktatvAt.h | ata ubhayAnuguNyAdasyAH prathamaprAptiH | ityatra shlokadvaye yadishabdadvayaM nivarteteti liN^.hprayogadvayaM cha | upalakShaNaM chaitat.h | vidyetetyapi grAhyam.h | tathA kenachiditi | satyatAmityupalakShaNam.h | anAditAM cheti grAhyam.h | AhurityavagamayantItyarthaH | tathAcha vishvamithyAtvaparatayA vyAkhyAne tadanupapattiriti sheShaH | yadyatra prapaJNchamithyAtvamabhi(saM)dhitsitaM syAttadA yo.ayaM prapaJNcho vidyata iva dR^ishyate sa nivartiShyate | aj~nAnena kalpito vikalpo vinivartiShyata iti vaktavyam.h | yadyAdyAstushabdA vigatArthA viruddhArthAshcha | tatprayoge hi prasaN^gadvayaparametadvAkyadvayamiti vij~nAyate | yadi parvato niragniko bhavet.h tarhi nirdhUmo.api syAditi yathA |

SUDHA_3.ACIHyadi cha jaDajIvabhedo nivarteta tadA jIvAnAM jaDatvApattyA mokShashAstravaiyarthyamityAdirUpeNa nivartetetyasyAniShyatvaM draShyavyam.h | na saMshaya itrata vyAptenirshchAyakamAha | evaM bhedapaJNchakasyAnAditAmupapAdya satyatAyAM pramANamAha- mAyAmAtramiti || yasmAdidaM prapaJNchashabdoktaM dvaitamuktarItyA mAyAmAtraM tasmAtsatyam.h | na hyavidyamAnamIshvarapraj~nAviShayo bhavati | bhrAntitvaprasaN^gAt.h | nApyavidyamAnaM kenApi rakShyate | atra dvayorbhAvo dvitA | tadIyo vargo dvaitam.h | sAmAnye napuMsakam.h | prapaJNchasambandhastu prakaraNAllabhyata iti j~nAtavyam.h | tarhyadvaitassarvabhAvAnAmityAdi kathamuktamityata Aha- advaitamiti || yadidaM parameshvarasyAdvaitatvaM(cha) visheShaNamuktaM na tat.h dvitIyavasturAhityAbhiprAyeNa | kintu paramArthataH | lyablopanimittA paJNchamI | uktamamarthamabhipretyeti | saptamyarthe vA tasiH | uttamArthaviShaya iti | bhedasatyatA.anaN^gIkAre bAdhakaM chAha- vikalpa iti || vikalpaH prakR^ito bhedo yadi kenachidaj~nAnAdinA kalpitaH syAttarhi chandrabhedavannivarteta | bAdhyeta | nacha bAdhyate | tasmAnna kalpitaH | kintu satya eveti | upasaMharati- upadeshAditi || tadevamupadeshAchChatyAdyanusAritvAt.h ayameva satAM vAdaH | yo bhedasatyatvAdiviShayaH | dvaitaM na vidyata iti tu tattve.aj~nAte sati bhavati | ato durvAda iti |

SUDHA_3.ACIHnanu cha sAN^ketikAnAmanAmutpattivinAshavattvaM saMskR^itanAmnAmanAdinityatvaM kimarthamatrochyate | paramaprakR^ite brahmavij~nAnena

SUDHA_3.ACIHyadapyuktaM j~nAnechChAprayatnasthAnakaraNapATavAni tAvadupadeshamAtreNa nishchIyanta iti | tanna | apaTukaraNAnAmapyupadeshadarshanena vyabhichArAdityAha- vyabhicharata iti || upadeshavisheShaNe chokto doShaH | nishchIyatAM j~nAnam.h, tasya yAthArthyaM tu kutaH | abhyAsadashApanno.ayam.h artho.asyeti sAmAnyanishchaye sati tatsiddhiriti netyAha- vyabhichArata iti || vyabhichAraH viprakarShaH teShAmeva sannidhAnaM durlabhamasmadAdInAM, dUre tadIyAbhyAsAvadhAraNamiti bhAvaH | vineyavachanaparamparayA tadavadhAraNamiti chet.h(na) | tIrthakarAntare vyabhichArAdityAha- vyabhichArata iti || tAsu tAsu smR^itiShvabhiniviShyAH sarve.api hi taM tamAchAryaM tatra tatrArthe.abhyAsavantamevAchakShate | nacha tadIyaM j~nAnaM yathArthamevAN^gIkartuM shakyaM, tvatsiddhAntavirodhitvAt.h | anyathA tvadIyasiddhAntasyAvAstavatvApAtAdityAha- vyabhichArata iti || vyabhichAraH virodhaH | ichChA.api vipralipsA kuto neti vAchyam.h | svopakAraparApakArarUpahetudarshanAbhAvAditi chet.h tatkiM smR^itipraNetArassarve.api na vipralambhakAH | addheti chet.h | asya niyamasya buddhAdiShu bhagnatvAdityAha- vyabhicharata iti || niyame cha svavyAghAtaH | yasya kasyApi vipralambhakatve, hetudarshanAbhAvasya tatraiva vyabhichAraH | nahi tattatpuruShavisheShAnusaMhitAste te prayojanavisheShAH pishitanayanairasmadAdibhiravadhArayituM shakyanta ityAshayenAha- vyabhichArata iti || kenApi pramANena hetUpalambhAbhAvo.avipralambhaheturiti chenna | sandigdhatvAt.h | prayojanAbhAvo.avipralambhahetuH | prayojanAbhAvashcha paravaJNchanasyApuruShArthatvAdatatsAdhanatvAchcha nishchIyata iti chenna | sampratipannavipralambhakeShu vyabhichArAdityAha- vyabhichArata iti || apuruShArthamapi puruShArthatayA vibhramya vaJNchayatyasAviti chet.h | kiM tAvatA | prakR^itastu vivekitayA naivamiti chenna | tIrthakarAntare avidyamAnasya vivekasyAsminnavadhAraNAnupapatteH |

SUDHA_4.ACIHdvividhA hi dharmA bhavanti | kechitparasparaparihAreNaiva vatarmAnAH | yathA kR^itakatvanityatve, svAtantyapAratante chetyevamAdayaH | kechitsamAviShyAH | te.api trividhAH | kechitsaN^kIrNAH | parasparaparihAreNaiva vartamAnayorekatra samAveshaH saN^karaH | yathA bhUtatvamUrtatve, puruShatvapAchakatve chetyevamAdayaH | kechitparAparabhAvAvasthitAH | yathA sattvadravyatve, dhUmavattvAgnimattve chetyevamAdayaH | kechittulyavR^ittayaH | yathA kR^itakatvAnityatve, gurutvarasavattve chetyA(tyevamA)dayaH | tatrAdyAnAM parasparasambandha eva nAstIti nAnumAnAnumeyabhAvaH | viruddhasamAkhyayA te.abhidhIyante | dvitIyAnAmapi satyapi sambandhe parasparavyabhichAreNa vyApyavyApakabhAvAbhAvAnnAnumAnAnumeyatA | kintu parasparamanaikAntikatayA.abhidhIyate | tR^itIyeShvapareShAM vyApyatayApareShAM vyApakatayA.astyanumAnAnumeyatvam.h | pare tvavyApyatayA nApareShvanumAnatAmashnute | kinnAmAnaikAntikA eva | chaturthAstu parasparaM vyApyavyApakabhAvAdanyonyamanumAnatAmarhantaH prasiddhayaprasiddhibhyAM vishiShyanta iti saN^kShepaH |

SUDHA_5.ACIHtatra sAmAnyamantyavisheShashcha samavAyashchetyetattrayaM nityamakAryaM cha | visheSha ityevoktte dravyaguNakarmasAmAnyAnAmapi grahaNaM syAt.h | vishiShyate.aneneti hi visheShaH | dravyaM cha daNDAdikamadaNDyAdibhyo devadattAdikaM vyAvartayati | guNashcha nirguNAd.hdravyam.h | kamarApi niShkriyAnmUrtam.h | sAmAnyaM dvividhaM paramaparaM cha | paraM sattA prachurAshrayatvAt.h | aparaM dravyatvAdi alpAshrayatvAt.h | tatra parasAmAnyasyAnuvR^ittimAtrahetutvena sAmAnyamAtratve.apyaparasAmAnyaM vyAvR^itterapi hetutvAdvisheSho.api ye vyAvartakA bhavanti te.antyAH | atyantavyAvR^ittihetava iti yAvat.h | nahi daNDAdikaM tathA | daNDyantarAdibhyo.avyAvartakatvAt.h |
SUDHA_5.ACIHguNA dravyANi cha nityAnityabhedena dvividhAnIti | tathAhi | dravyANi pR^ithivyaptejovAyvAkAshakAlAdigAtmamanAMsi | tatra paramANurUpANi pR^ithivyAdIni chatvAri, gaganAdIni paJNcha nityAni | dvayaNukAdirUpANi pR^ithivyAdIni chatvAryanityAnIti | guNAshchAnityadravyagatA anityA eva | pArthivaparamANAvaikatvaikapR^ithaktavaparimANagurutvAni nityAni  | rUparasagandhasparshAnekatvAnekapR^ithaktavasaMyogavibhAgaparatvAparatvasaMskArA anityAH | (Apye cha) pAthasIye cha rUparasasparshaikatvaikapR^ithaktavaparimANagurutvadravyatvasnehA nityAH | anekatvAnekapR^ithaktavasaMyogavibhAgaparatvAparatvasaMskArA anityAH | taijase cha rUpasparshaikatvaikapR^ithaktavaparimANAni nityAni | anekatvAnekapR^ithaktvasaMyogavibhAgaparatvadravyatvasaMskArA anityAH | vAyavIye cha sparshaikatvaikapR^ithaktavaparimANAni nityAni | anekatvAnekapR^ithaktavasaMyogavibhAgaparatvAparatvasaMskArA anityAH | AkAshe chaikatvaikapR^ithaktavaparimANAni nityAni | aketvAnekapR^ithaktavasaMyogavibhAgashabdA anityAH | kAle dishi chaikatvaikapR^ithaktavaparimANAni nityAni | anekatvAnekapR^ithaktavasaMyogavibhAgA anityAH | Atmani chaikatvaikapR^ithaktavaparimANAni nityAni | anekatvAnekapR^ithaktavasaMyogavibhAgA buddhayAdayashcha nava anityAH | IshvarasyApi visheSho.abhihitaH | manasi chaikatvaikapR^ithaktavaparimANAni nityAni | anekatvAnekapR^ithaktavasaMyogavibhAgaparatvAparatvasaMskArA anityAH | iti vivekaH | 
SUDHA_5.ACIHAdyastushabdo dravyAdvisheShaM dyotayati | dvitIyasya dravyakAraNaM tvityanvayaH | yadvA dvAvapyanukttasamuchchayArthau | tachchokttam.h | tathAhi | kAryagatAnAM rUparasagandhasparshaparimANaikatvaikapR^ithaktavottarasaMyogavibhAgagurutvadravatvasnehavegAnAM kAraNagatA rUpAdayo.asamavAyikAraNam.h | pArthivaparamANugatAnAM rUparasagandhasparshAnAM pArthivataijasaparamANugatadravyasya tadgata eva tejaH saMyogaH | sarvatrAnekatvAnekapR^ithaktavayorAshrayagataikatvaikapR^ithaktavAni | saMyogavibhAgavegAnAmAshrayagataM karma | paratvAparatvayorAshrayagatau dikkAlasaMyogau | AtmavisheShaguNAnAmAtmagato manaH saMyogaH | shabdasyAkAshagatAH saMyogavibhAgashabdAH | karmaNashchAshrayagatA gurutvadravatvavegasaMyogA iti | dravyasya tu samavAyikAraNAnAmavayavAnAM saMyogo.asamavAyikAraNamiti | 
SUDHA_5.ACIHchaturvidhaM parimANam.h | aNutvaM mahattvaM hrasvatvaM dIrghatvaM cha | tatrANutvaM dvividhaM, nityamanityaM cha | nityaM chaturvidhaparamANau manasi cha | pArimANDalyamiti chochyate | anityaM dvayaNuka eva | mahattvamapi dvividhaM nityAnityabhedAt.h | nityamAkAshakAladigAtmasu paramamahattvam.h | anityaM tyaNukAdau kAyardravye | hrasvatvaM dvayaNuka eva | dIrghatvaM tyaNukAdikAryadravya eva | kechitparamANAvapi hrasvatvaM gaganAdAvapi dIrghatvamabhyupayanti | tatra dvayaNuke vartamAnaM hrasvatvam.h | upalakShaNametat.h | aNutvaM cha kAryaguNe dvayaNukakAryatyaNukaparimANe | viShayasaptamIyam.h | tyaNukamahaddIrghatvayorasamavAyikAraNaM na bhavati | tathA paramANau vartamAnaM parimaNDalaM pArimANDalyaM paramANukAryadvayaNukaguNasya hrasvatvasyANutvasya chAsamavAyikAraNaM na bhavati | tyaNukAdigataM tu mahattvaM dIrghatvaM cha chaturaNukAdiparimANaM pratyasamavAyikAraNaM bhavatyeveti | 
SUDHA_5.ACIHtatra dvayaNukaparamANuparimANAnAM tyaNukadvayaNukaparimANAni prati kAraNatvAbhAve vairUpyaM vijAtIyatvaM kAraNam.h | sajAtIyayoreva hi tantupaTaparimANayoH kAryakAraNabhAvo dR^iShyaH | tathAcha prayogaH | dvayaNukatyaNukaparimANe na kAryakAraNabhAvavatI vijAtIyaparimANatvAt.h | vyatirekeNa tantupaTaparimANavat.h | evaM paramANudvayaNukaparimANayorapi draShyavyam.h | paramANoraNutvaM dvayaNukANutvasya kAraNamastviti chenna | tatrApi nityaparimANatvasya paramANutvasya cha vairUpyasya sattvAt.h | evaJNchedvayaNukatyaNukaparimANAnAM kimasamavAyikAraNamityata Aha- vairUpyamiti || anekatvamityarthaH | IshvarabuddhimapekShyotpannA paramANvordvitvasaN^khayA dvayaNuke.aNutvaM hrasvatvaM cha karoti | dvayaNukeShu chotpannA tritvasaN^khayA tyaNuke mahattvaM dIrghatvaM cha karotIti | 
SUDHA_5.ACIHetadukttaM bhavati | tyaNukAdvayaNukaparimANaM svAshrayAshrayasamavAyikAraNaparimANajam.h kAryaparimANattvAchchaturaNukAdiparimANavat.h, dvayaNukaparamANuparimANaM parimANArambhakaM dravyasamavAyikAraNaparimANatvAt.h, tyaNukaparimANavat.h tyaNukadvayaNuke vA parimANArabhyaparimANavatI kAryadravyatvAchchaturaNukAdivat.h, dvayaNukaparamANU parimANAsamavAyikAraNaparimANavantau dravyasamavAyikAraNatvAt.h tyaNukavaditi | nacha vivakShitArthAsiddhiH, anyathA.anupapattyA tatsiddheH | nacha yatra kevalena prachayena parimANamArabhyate tatra vyabhichAra iti vAchyam.h, tasyApi pakShatulyatvAt.h | nachaivaM sati bAdhaH, prachayakAraNatAyA anivAraNAt.h | nachobhayakAraNatvakalpane gauravadoShaH, dvayorapi klR^iptashakttitvAt.h | dvayaNukaparimANaM tyaNukaparimANAjanakam.h, paramANuparimANaM cha dvayaNukaparimANAjanakam.h, parimANatvAt.h paTaparimANavat.h, ityAdinA 
SUDHA_5.ACIHsatpratipakShateti chenna, tatsamavAyikANaparimANatvAbhAvasyopAdhitvAt.h, tyaNukaparimANaM chaturaNukaparimANAjanakam.h parimANatvAtpaTaparimANavat.h, ityAdyAbhAsasamAnayogakShematvAchcha | paramANuparimANaM parimANAnArambhakaM nityaparimANatvAt.h gaganaparimANavadityapi na, dravyasamavAyikAraNaparimANatvAbhAvasyopAdhitvAt.h | apyaparamANurUpaM rUpAnArambhakaM nityatvAt.h gaganaparimANavat.h, paramANavo dravyAnArambhakA nityatvAdgaganavat.h, ityAdyAbhAsatulyatvAchcha | 
SUDHA_5.ACIHetena paramANudvayaNukaparimANe parimANAnArambhake aNutvAnmanaHparimANavadityapi parAstam.h | na chAnaNutvamupAdhiH | vakShyamANanyAyena parimANAvAntarajAterapAkaraNAt.h | pakShIkR^itAd.hghrasvatvAdavyAvR^itteshcha |
SUDHA_5.ACIHnanu cha tyaNukAdiparimANaM chaturaNukAdiparimANaM cha sajAtIyamiti yukttastatra kAryakaraNabhAvaH | dvayaNukatyaNukaparimANayostu vijAtIyatvAtkathaM tathAtvamityato dR^iShyAntadArShyAntikayoH sadR^ishamityukttam.h | yathA tyaNukAdiparimANAchchaturaNukAdau sajAtIyaM parimANamutpadyate | tathA dvayaNukaparamANuparimANAdapi tyaNukAdau sajAtIyaparimANotpAdasyaiva sisAdhayiShitatvAnna doSha ityarthaH | 
SUDHA_5.ACIHnanu cha dvayaNukAdiparimANasya paramANvAdiparimANAjanyatve bAdhakAbhAvAdaprayojakatvamanumAnAnAm.h | dvayaNukAdiparimANasya saN^khayaiva janmasambhavAdityAshaN^kAM pariharan.h vAshabdaM vyAkhyAti- nachediti ||
SUDHA_5.ACIHsadR^ishaparimANasyaiva kAraNatvAvadhAraNAdvisadR^ishametadakAraNamavarjanIyasannidhIti chet.h | kimidaM visadR^ishatvam.h | kiM jAtibhedaH | uta vailakShaNyamAtram.h | nAdyaH | paramANudvayaNukAdiparimANAnAmanumAnenaikajAtIyatvasyApi sAdhitatvAt.h | dvitIye vailakShaNyamAtreNa na chetkAraNatvaM tadA mahattvAderapi na syAt.h | nahi tyaNukachaturaNukamahattve na vilakShaNe | sotkarShatvasyAnubhavasiddhatvAt.h | 
SUDHA_5.ACIHatha saN^khayAta eva janmasambhave parimANasyApi kAraNatvaM na kalpanIyamiti chet.h | tathA.apyuktta evAtiprasaN^gaH | chaturaNukAdiparimANasyApi saN^khayAta eva jananopapatteH | yatra tu niyAmakavisheShastatra parimANamapyAdriyatAmiti | yadyapi pariNAmavAdinAM nAyaM panthAH | kintUpAdAnAni svaguNayukttAni tathAvidhakAryatAmApadyanta iti | tathA.api paramatamAshritya pa(reShAmevedaM)rasyedaM dUShaNAbhidhAnamiti na kAchitkShatiH |
SUDHA_5.ACIHevaM paramANuparimANAd.hdvayaNukaparimANasyotpAdaH tatastyaNukaparimANasya janma teShAM chaikajAtIyatvamityanumAnena sAdhitam.h | tadasat.h | pratitarkaparAhatatvAt.h | tathAhi | kiM paramANuparimANAdvayaNuke dvayaNukaparimANAchcha tyaNuke sajAtIyaparimANasyANutvasyotpattiH sAdhyate uta mahattvasya atha hrasvatvasya yadvA dIrghatvasya | sarveShAmapi pakShANAM duShyatvaM pratijAnIte- sadR^ishasya hIti ||
SUDHA_5.ACIHyadi paramANuparimANAdaNutvena sajAtIyaM dvayaNuke, dvayaNukaparimANAchcha tyaNuke parimANamutpadyate | tadA 
SUDHA_5.ACIHdvitIye tu paramANudvayaNukayorapi mahattve pratyakShatvApattiH | na chodbhUtarUpasparshayoranyatarAbhAvena tadabhAvaH | tyaNukAdAvapi tadA(dabhAvA)patteH | ata eva chaturtho.api parAstaH | dIrghatve mahatvasyAvarjanIyatvAditi pakShadvayadUShaNaM spaShyatvAnnokttam.h | yadyapIdaM parimANAvAntarajAtInAmaNutvAdInAmaprAmANikatvoktayA parihR^itameva | tathA.api tasyaivArthasya sphuTIkaraNArthaM punarAshaN^kitamityadoShaH | 
SUDHA_5.ACIHyadukttaM kimaNutvasyotpattiH sAdhyata ityAdi, tatra paramANumahattvAd.hdvayaNuke mahattvam.h | dvayaNukamahattvAttyaNukamahattvamutpadyate ityeSha pakShastAvatparigR^ihyata ityarthaH | yadyapyatra parimANAvAntarajAtyabhAvAnnaivaM vikalpa eva yujyata iti vakttavyam.h, tathA.api tadabhAvamevopapAdayituM gUDhAbhisandhinA pakShaparigrahaH kR^ita iti j~nAtavyam.h | 
SUDHA_5.ACIHparamANoraNutvAd.hdvayaNuke.aNutvaM dvayaNukANutvAttyaNuke.aNutvaM tatashcha chaturaNuke.aNutvamiti vA pakShaH parigR^ihyata iti bhAvaH | nanvevaM sati pakShadvayokttadoShApattirvyAghAtashchAdhikaH | tathA hi | paramANumArabhyAntyAvayaviparyantasyodbhUta(rUpa)sparshavato mahattve sarvasyApi pratyakShatvaM syAt.h | aNutve chApratyakShatvaM syAt.h | nacha paramANvAdeH pratyakShatvaM tyaNukAderapratyakShatvaM yukttam.h | pratyakShatvApratyakShatve cha parasparavyAhate | yatpratyakShaM ghaTAdi na tadapratyakSham.h | yachchApratyakShaM gaganAdi na tatpratyakShamiti tayoH parasparaparihAreNaiva vR^itteH | 
SUDHA_5.ACIHparamANvAdAvakhile.api dravye pratyakShatvApratyakShatve sta eveti naitau prasaN^gau yukttau | nacha vyAhatiH | puruShabhedApekShayA vyavasthopapatteriti | etachchottaratra sphuTIbhaviShyati | 
SUDHA_5.ACIHetadukttaM bhavati | syAdayaM paramANvAdiShvakhiladravyeShvaNutvamahattvAN^gIkAre virodho yadi rUpe nIlatvapItatvavatparimANe.aNutvamahattvAdijAtiyogaH syAt.h | nachaivam.h | pramANAbhAvAt.h | kintu yathA tyaNukAdiShu mahattvamekajAtIyameva, utkarShApakarShavatpareNAN^gIkR^itam.h | yathAchANutvaM paramANudvayaNukayoH | evaM parimANamavAntarajAtirahitameva sarvadravyeShUtkarShApakarShavadvartate | tathA chaikatra dravye vartamAnaM parimANaM dravyAntaravartyutkR^iShyaparimANApekShayA.aNutvamityuchyate | tadeva dravyAntavartino.apakR^iShyaparimANasyApekShayA mahattvamityuchyate | evaJNcha kuto virodhaH | yathA khalvekameva dravyaM dravyabhedApekShayA sannikR^iShyaM viprakR^iShyaM chochyamAnaM na virodhAspadam.h | ata eva pratyakShatvApratyakShatvavirodho.apyapAstaH | tayormahattvAdimAtranimittatve hi sa syAt.h | na chaivam.h | kintu puruShANAmindriyapATavanimittatvameva | anyathA mandavilochanenApi tyaNukamupalabhyeta | tarhi gaganAderapi kadAchitpratyakShatvaM syAditi chenna | udbhUtarUpAbhAvAt.h | dvayaNukAnupalambho guNavisheShaviparyayAdhInaH AlokendriyasannikR^iShyachAkShuShadravyAnupalambhatvAt.h | pavanAnupalambhavadityAdikaM tvapakR^iShyamahattvAdinaivAnyathAsiddham.h | tarhi parvatAderapratyakShatA syAt.h iti chenna | apakarShavisheShasya vivakShitatvAt.h | nAsau vyavasthito.astIti chet.h | satyam.h | ata eva puruShApekShayetyukttamiti | 
SUDHA_5.ACIHastvevaM parimANe.avAntarajAtyabhAvastathA.api na sarvatra mahattvANutvabhyupagamo yujyate | utkR^iShyApakR^iShyaparimANApekShayA hi madhyavarti parimANamaNutvaM mahattvaM chochyata ityukttam.h | tachcha dvayaNukAdiparimANe sambhavati | nacha paramANuparimANe | nahi 
SUDHA_5.ACIHparamANuparimANAdapakR^iShyaM parimANamasti | yadapekShayA tanmahattvaM syAt.h | ataH paramANoraNutvameva | tathAcha na mahattvaM chetyasadityata Aha- tAratamyeti ||
SUDHA_5.ACIHyasmAtsarve.api padArthAH parimANatAratamyenaiva sthitAH | svaparimANApekShayotkR^iShyApakR^iShyaparimANavantaH | sarvANyapi dravyANi kutashchitparimANAdutkR^iShyena parimANena upetAnIti vA | tasmAtparamANorapi mahattvaM yujyate iti sambandhaH | ayamatra prayogaH | paramANuH kutashchidutkR^iShyena parimANena yukttaH, svaparimANApekShayA.apakR^iShyaparimANavAniti vA, dravyatvAttantuvaditi | nacha paramANorapakR^iShyadravyAbhAvAdbAdhitaviShayatvam.h | tadbhAgAnAM vakShyamANatvAt.h | nacha teShveva vyabhichAraH | teShAmapi bhAgavattvAt.h | 
SUDHA_5.ACIHtadevaM paramANudvayaNukAdiparimANAnAM vaijAtyasyAbhAvAdyukttaM sautramanumAnamiti siddham.h | yadyapi vaijAtyamaN^gIkR^ityApi kAryakAraNabhAvaH shakyopapAdanaH | anyathA saN^khayAyA apyakAraNatvApatteH | parimANasyaivamiti niyamasya nirmUlatvAt.h | tathA.api vastusthitireva vakttavyeti | parimANatvAvAntarajAtyapAkaraNena sajAtIyatAmupapAdyAnumAnaM samAhitamiti j~nAtavyam.h |
SUDHA_5.ACIHparamANorapyutkR^iShyaparimANAshrayatvamukttaM tadAkShipati- yatheti ||
SUDHA_5.ACIHparimANatvata iti || parimAratAratamyatvAdityarthaH | tatAchANau siddhe.aNutvasiddhistatsiddhau cha tat.h(aNutva)siddhiriti parasparAshrayadoShaH parAstaH | tadayamarthaH | parimANApakarShatAratamyaM kvachidvishrAntaM parimANatAratamyatvAt.h parimANotkarShatAratamyavadityanumAnena parimANApakarShatAratamyasya kvachidvishrAntisiddhau yatredaM vishrAntaM yataH paramANurnAsti sa paramANuriti parimANApakarShakAShThAshrayatayA siddhasya paramANoH kathamutkR^iShyaparimANAkhyamapi mahattvaM sAdhayituM shakyam.h | dharmigrAhakapramANena svavachanena (cha) vyAghAtAditi |
SUDHA_5.ACIHmahattvamiti dravyavisheShasyevaM (syaiva) saMj~nA | tena Anmahata ityeSha vidhirna bhavati | "dR^iShyAnugatirhi saMj~nAChandasoH' iShyate | yathA.a.aha "bahulaM taNi' iti | guNashabdo.atra tantreNa dviH upAttaH | tatrAdyasya parimANAkhyo guNavisheSho.arthaH | dvitIyasya guNanam.h Ishvara iti paramamahattvAshrayadravyopalakShaNam.h | parimANotkarShatAratamyasyeyattAparichChedo hi tathA sati dR^iShyaH syAt.h | yadi mahattattvAdiparimANagaNanayeshvarAdiH etAvAnpaJNchaguNaparimANavAn.h ShaD.hguNaparimANavAnveti parichChinnaH syAt.h | nachaivam.h | tathA sati paramamahattvAnupapatteriti hishabdArthaH | 
SUDHA_5.ACIHatra mahattattvagrahaNenedaM sUchayati | yadukttaM vaisheShikAdibhiH pR^ithivyAdIni navaiva dravyANi iti tadasat.h | mahadahaN^kArAdInAmapi sattvAt.h | nacha tatra pramANAbhAvaH | shrutyAdeH pramANasya vidyamAnatvAt.h | nacha tyaNukAdikameva tathochyate | avyakttatvAdishravaNAt.h | nacha bAdhakaM kiJNchit.h vidyate | yenopachArakalpaneti | IshvaragrahaNena jIvAtmanAmapi yatparaiShaH paramamahattvamukttaM tadasaditi sUchayati | upapAdayiShyate khalvaNutvaM jIvasyeti | 
SUDHA_5.ACIHtarhIti sheShaH | kashchiditi vartate | evaM sAdhane kashchidapi dravyavisheSho nAvasAyayituM shakyaH | ayameva sarvato.apakR^iShyaparimANavAnnAto.apakR^iShyaparimANo.astIti sarvAntimatayA na pratipattuM kashchichChakyate | kutaH kevalaM sAkShAdvirodhAt.h | parimANApakarSho.anantashcha paryavasitashcheti hi vipratiShiddhametat.h | bhavitavyaM chAvasAnena | anyathA sarvasyApyutkR^iShyApakR^iShyaparimANasambhavena paramANormahattvanirAkaraNAsambhavAt.h | evashabdena virodhasyAparihAryatvaM sUchayati | tadanenApasiddhAnto.abhihito bhavati | 
SUDHA_5.ACIHyadi chAnantyamavadhIrya parimANApakarShatAratamyaM kvachidAshritamityeva pratij~nArthaH syAt.h | tathA.api na sisA(ShA)dhayiShitamavasAnaM labhyata ityarthAntaratA syAt.h | yathA.a.akAshAderutkR^iShyaparimANaM dravyaM nAsti tathA paramANorapakR^iShyaparimANaM dravyaM nAstIti tAtparyArthaM iti chet.h | satyam.h | nAyamito labhyata iti uchyate | parimANApakaShartAratamyaM kvachinniratishayam.h parimANatAratamyatvAtparimANotkaShartAratamyavaditi vivakShitamiti chet.h | ko.ayamatishayo nAma | kimAdhikyamuta nyUnatA | atha sAdhAraNaM kiJNchit.h | Adye bAdhaH | dvitIye dR^iShyAntasya sAdhyavikalatA | na tR^itIyaH | tadabhAvAt.h | shabdasAmyamAtreNAnumAnApravR^itteH | yathA.a.akAshAdiparimANamubhayAvadhimanna bhavati | tathA tyaNukAvayavAvayavaparimANamapi sAdhyamiti chenna | hetvabhAvAt.h | parimANatvasya ghaTAdiparimANe vyabhichArAt.h | nityaparimANatvasyAshrayAnityatAyA vakShyamANatvenAsiddheH | parimANakAShThatvasya cha sAdhyatvAt.h | evaM tAtparyAntarANyapi nirAkAryANIti | 
SUDHA_5.ACIHparimANotkarShatAratamyasyAnantatvaM dR^ishyata ityukttam.h | tatkena pramANenetyAshaN^kaya kAlAkAsheshvarAdIni hi dravyANi paramamahattvayantIShyante | tatra kAlAkAshayostAvatparimANotkarShasyAnantyaM sAkShisiddhamityAha- kevalamiti ||

SUDHA_5.ACIHmahattvAtkathamasau paramANuriti chenna | mahattvAsiddheH | chAkShuShadravyatvAttatsiddhiriti chenna | kasyachidamahato.api chAkShuShatve bAdhakAbhAvAt.h | mahattvaM cha dravyachAkShuShatAyAM kAraNamiti chet.h | satyam.h | kvachidanyadapi kAraNaM kalpayiShyate | gauravaM tathA sati syAditi chenna | dharmikalpanAto dharmamAtrakalpanAyAH laghutvAt.h | astu vA mahattvam.h | tathA.apyaNutvena tasya samAveshe ko virodhaH | kAryatvasAdhanaM chAprayojakam.h | mahato.apyAtmanaH pratyakShavachchAkShuShatvopapatteH | paramamahattvAbhAvena kriyAsambhavAchcha | mahattvasya kAraNabahutvaM kAraNamiti chenna | nityatvopapatteH | chAkShuShamahattvAnneti chenna | bAdhakAbhAvAt.h | ata eva kAryadravyatvamasiddham.h | santu vA tadavayavAsta eva paramANava iti teShAM punaravayavasAdhanAya pakShIkartumashakyatvAtkuta evAnumA bhavet.h | nanu mahad.hdravyArambhakatvAtte.api sAvayavA eveti chenna | niravayavasya ma(hA)had.hdravyArambhakatve bAdhakAbhAvAt.h | bahutvenaiva mahattvArambhopapatteH | dravyArambhe sAvayavatsyAnupayogAt.h | santu vA dvayaNukAvayavAste.api kutaH paramANavaH | mahad.hdravyArambhakatvena teShAmapi sAvayavatvAnumAnAt.h | anavasthA bAdhiketi chenna | tadavayavAnAM tadavayavAvayavAnAM vA niravayavatvena tadvishrAnteH | kathaM cheyamanavasthA dUShaNam.h | merusarShapAdInAM samaparimANatvApattistu dUShitA | ghaTAdikAryAnutpattiriti chenna | sAvayavasyaiva nityatvopapatteH | yathokttam.h | avibhAgaH pa(raNu)ramANuteti |
SUDHA_5.ACIHevaM paramANudvayaNukayoranumAnataH siddhimapAkR^itya prasaN^gAdAkAshAdiparimANotkarShAnantyasyAnumAnikatvaM na yujyata iti yadukttaM tatprapaJNchayati- deshAntareti ||
SUDHA_5.ACIHsampratipannadeshAdinA sadR^ishaM sajAtIyaM (chA)vA.asmatpakShe gaganAdiparimANotkarShAnantyamanabhyupagachChatAM pakShe kimeva na bhavati | kintu bhavatyeveti | tathAcha sampratipannadeshasya tataH sthUlenAtmanA sadR^ishena sajAtIyena vopetatvasya siddhatvAtsiddhasAdhanatA syAt.h | AkAshAdiparimANotkarShAnantyAsiddherarthAntaratA cheti | sampratipannadeshasyeshvarAdimattvaM bAdhitaM sambandhAbhAvAditi chenna | deshAntareNApi sambandhAbhAvAt.h | etena shashaviShANAdisAdhakAnumAne.api bAdhAbhidhAnaM parAstam.h | deshAntarAnumAne.api sAmyAt.h | tadevaM paramANudvayaNukayorAkAshAdiparimANotkarShAntyasya cha sAkShisiddhatAmanaN^gIkR^itya kevalAnumAnavedyatvasvIkaraNamanupapannamityukttam.h | 
SUDHA_5.ACIHvAshabdaH samuchchaye | apiranumAnasya samuchchayArthaH | niyAmako grAhakaH | mAnam.h anumAnamAnatvopayoginI | anyA pratyakShAdyagR^ihItA | sandigdhamUlataH sandigdha(gdhA)vyabhichAratvataH | avyabhichAro hi sAhityasya vyAptitve mUlam.h | tatra pratyakShagR^ihItA vyAptiryathA dhUmasyAgninA | AgamagR^ihItA yathA | brAhmaNo na hantavya iti | anumAnagR^ihItA yathA | vyatirekiprayoge | etadukttaM bhavati | pratyakShAdyavadhR^itaM hi vyAptyAdi anumAnamAnA(natA)N^gam.h | na svayamAtrasiddham.h | sandigdha(gdhA)vyabhichA(ra)ritvAt.h | samayAnAM sandigdhamUlatvAchcha | vidyate cha dhUmAdyanumAnAnAM pramANAvadhR^itaM vyAptyAdIti na pratibandIgrahamAtreNa tadbhaN^gaH | na paramANvAdyanumAnAnAmiti pratibandIgrastatvAdaprAmANyameva | nanu vyAptyAdyabhAve kiM pratibandIgraheNa | tata evAprAmANyasiddheriti | satyam.h | pratyakShAdyanavadhR^itavyAptyAderapi prAmANye.atiprasaN^go vA tadaprAmANye dR^iShyAnto vA pratibandIgraheNa dyotyata ityadoSha iti |
SUDHA_5.ACIHsatyametatpratyakShAdyavadhR^itaiva vyAptiranumAnaprAmANyopayoginIti | sA cha dhUmAnumAvatparamANvAdyanumAneShvapyastyeva | dhUmasyAgnineva mahadArambhakatvAdInAmapi sAvayavatvAdinA sAhityadarshanAdityata Aha- saheti || 
SUDHA_5.ACIHnanvanenaiva nyAyena mahadArambhakatvAdInAmapi vyAptinishchayasambhavAtkathaM paramANvAdAvanumAnApravR^ittiriti chenna | pakShetaratvasyopAdhitvasambhavena vyabhichArAbhAvAnishchayAt.h | atha tasyopAdhitvaM nAstItyuchyeta dAta bAdhakamAha- anyatheti || 
SUDHA_5.ACIHpakShetaratvasyopAdhitAmanAdR^itya pramANAntarAsahakR^itenaivAnumAnena paramANvAdisiddhayabhyupagama ityarthaH | madhuro raso lavaNAdirasapaJNchakavyatirikttarasAnyonyAbhAvavAn.h rasatvAllavaNAdityAdyanumayA | aniShyAni cha sarvANi dahanashaityAdInyApateyuH | kutaH | yasmAdevaMvidhAnumA kAmachAriNI | nanu cha saptamarasAderanupalambhAdibAdhitatvAtpakShetaratvopAdhiduShyatvamanumAnAnAmiti chetsamaM prakR^ite.api | paramANvAderapyanupalambhabAdhitatvAt.h | ayogyaM taditi chet.h | tulyaM saptamarasAdAvapi | anumAnaprAmANye saptamarasAdisiddhAvayogyatvaM kalpyam.h | kalpite cha tasminnanumAnaprAmANyasiddhirityanyonyAshrayatvamiti chet.h | etadapi tAdR^igeva | anupabhogyasya saptamarasAdeH kalpane gauravamiti chet.h | samAdhisAmyam.h | pramite na gauravaM doSha ityetadapi samAnam.h | tasmAtparamANvAdeH sAkShivedyatvamaN^gIkR^itya pratibandI mochanIyeti kathaM na tasya sAkShivedyatvamiti |
SUDHA_5.ACIHsaMyogatvaM sambandhavyAvR^ittam.h jAtitvAdgotvavaditi siddhasAdhanam.h | jAteH prativyakttiniyatatvasya vakShyamANatvenaikasya saMyogatvasya saMyogAntarAdvayAvR^itteH, visheShaNavisheShyabhAvAdito vyAvR^itteshcha | vivAdAdhyAsitA mR^it.h ghaTasambaddhA dravyatvAdAkAshavaditi cha ghaTAntarasaMyogenArthAntaram.h | etadghaTasambaddheti nirdeshe.apyetadghaTasambandhamalabdhvA vinaShyadravye.anaikAntikam.h | tatrApi paramparAsambandho.astIti chet.h | tarhi siddhasAdhanam.h | mR^itsaMyukttabhUtalasya ghaTasaMyukttatvAt.h |
SUDHA_5.ACIHnanu dharmA dharmito bhinnA eva | nachokttadoShaH | naiyAyikAdibhiH paramANvArambhavAdibhiH ShaDeva padArthA iti niyamasyAnaN^gIkR^itatvAt.h | dharmapadArthasya pR^ithagaN^gIkR^itatvAchcha | tathAcha bhinnadharmasaMsargavashAtsarvavyavahAropapattau na tadanyathA.anupapattyA visheShasiddhirityata Aha- padArtheti ||
SUDHA_5.ACIHayamAshayaH | sAmAnyasyApi sAmAnyaM tAvatpareNa nAN^gIkR^itam.h | tathA guNasyApi guNo nAN^gIkR^itaH | tatkasmAditi vakttavyam.h | na tAvatpratItyabhAvAt.h | sadgotvaM chaturviMshatiguNA rUpAdrasaH pR^ithagiti pratibhAsasya durapahnavatvAt.h | nacha na sadgotvamityAdi bAdhakamasti yena pratItasyApi parityAgaH | gotvaM na sattAvadaparasAmAnyashUnyatvAdvisheShavat.h, guNA na guNavanto.adravyatvAtkriyAvadityAdibAdhakamastIti chenna | vipakShe bAdhakAbhAvenAprayojakatvAt.h | dR^iShyAntayoH(shcha)sAdhyavikalatvAchcha | yadi gotvAdau sattA syAttadA sattAyAmapi syAt.h | tathA chAtmAshrayatvamiti chenna | sattAntaratvopapatteH | kiJNcha pratIteH kimAtmAshrayatA kariShyati | anyathA prameyatvAdInAM kevalAnvayitvaM na syAt.h | AtmAshrayabhayAdyataH prameyatvAdivyAvR^ittiH tasyaiva vipakShatvAt.h | ukttaM cha "kathaM svavR^ittiriShyA chedyathA.anyatreti gR^ihyatAm.h | pramANaM sharaNaM vR^ittau na bhinnAbhinnateyatA' iti | guNAnAmapi guNavattve dravyalakShaNayogAd.hdravyatApattiriti chenna | pratItimanuruddhaya lakShaNAntarasya kartavyatvAt.h | tasmAtsAmAnye sAmAnyaM guNe cha guNaH anavasthAbhayAdeva nAN^gIkriyata ityeva vakttavyam.h | yathA.a.aha "vyaktterabhedastulyatvaM saN^karo.athAnavasthitiH | rUpahAnirasambandho jAtibAdhakasaN^grahaH' iti | nachAnavachChinnA sAmAnyaparamparA guNaparamparA chotpattij~naptipratibandhe hetuH | tathAcha yathA sA dUShaNaM tathA prakR^itA.api dUShaNameva | na chetsA.api na syAditi sAmAnyAderapi sAmAnyAdyaN^gIkAryaM syAt.h | yadi kathaJNchijj~naptipratibandhakatvaM tatra vyutpadyeta | tarhi vayamapyatra tad.hvyutpAdayiShyAma iti |
SUDHA_5.ACIHyadi kashchidvaiyAtyAdbrUyAt.h | astyeva sAmAnyasyApi sAmAnyaM guNasyApi guNo nirbAdhapratItisiddhatvAt.h | astyeva sAmAnyasyApi sAmAnyaM guNasyApi guNo nirbAdhapratItisiddhatvAt.h | utpattij~naptyapratibandhahetoranavasthAyA doShatvAyogAt.h | ato naitannyAyena dharmaparamparA.anavasthAbhayAnnivAraNIyeti | tatrAha- sa cheti ||
SUDHA_5.ACIHnanvaparyavasitaparamparAmAtrasAmye.api yatrotpattyAdipratibandhakatvaM tatra dUShaNatvam.h | yatra yadabhAvastatrAdUShaNatvamiti chet.h | kimarthamutpattyAdipratibandhakatvamanusaraNIyam.h | anavasthA hi tarkavisheShaH | tarkashchAniShyaprasaJNjanam.h | utpattyAdipratibandhashchAniShyaH | prAmANikaparityAgarUpatvAt.h | utpattyAdeH prAmANikatvAt.h | atastadapratibandhe tarkatvAyogAtkathaM dUShaNAntaram.h | evameva dUShaNatve.atiprasaN^ga ita chet.h | kiM prAmANikaparityAga evAniShya utAprAmANikasvIkAro.api | nAdyaH | niyAmakAbhAvAt.h | dvitIye kathaM na prakR^itAnavasthA dUShaNam.h | atyantabhinnadharmaparamparAyA apyaprAmANikatvAt.h | athAprAmANikasvIkAro na dUShaNam.h | tarhi prAmANikaparityAgo.api na (dUShaNaM) syAditi nAnavasthA kvachid.hdUShaNaM bhavet.h | athAniShyApattiheturanavasthAdUShaNam.h | na punaraniShyarUpeti chenna | aniShyarUpaivAnavasthA dUShaNam.h | natvaniShyApattiheturityapi vakttuM shakyatvena kvachidaN^gIkR^itA.apyanavasthA na dUShaNaM bhavet.h | tasmAtprAmANikaparityAgAprAmANikaparigraharUpA vA taddheturvA.anavachChinnaparamparA.anavastheti vAchyam.h | ata eva nAtiprasaN^gaH | tathAcha dharmaparamparAyA apyanavasthAtvenAbheda evAN^gIkAryaH | evaM chokttanyAyena vyavahArAnyathA.anupapattyA visheShasiddhiriti | 
SUDHA_5.ACIHdharmadharmiNoH savisheShAbhedavAdinAM pakSha ityarthaH | guNAdyA guNAH sAmAnyAni cha | tadvanto guNavantaH | sAmAnyavanti cha | tena chaturviMshatiguNAH sadgotvamityAdipratItivirodho nAstIti sheShaH | ananyatvAt.h dharmadharmiNoriti sheShaH | aprAmANikAparyavasitaparamparArUpA hyeShA | ananyatve kathaM tadvR^ittamiti tadavasthaH pratItivirodha ityata ukttam.h- visheShato hi tadvanta iti || bhedasambandhakAryakArI hi visheSha iti | 
SUDHA_5.ACIHsyAdetat.h | yathA bhedasAdhakAnAM vyapadeshabhedAdInAM visheShAshrayeNaivAnyathAsiddhirukttA | tathA satyapi tasminnasattvasyApi visheShaNaiva nirvAhaH kriyatAm.h | kiM bhedAbhedAbhyupagamena | maivam.h | visheShasya bhedakAryavyavahAramAtranirvAhakatvena vinAshaM pratyanirvAhakatvAt.h | sakalabhedakAyarkAritve visheSho bheda eva, na tatpratinidhiH syAt.h | kiJNchAnekAshritasyAvayavino dvitvAdeshchAshrayeNAtyAntAbhede satyAshrayaNAmapi parasparamabhedaH prasajyate | tatparihArArthaM tAvadavashyaM tatra bhedo.aN^gIkaraNIyaH | nachAvachChedakena vinA bhedAbhedabhUmeH saN^grahaH syAdityayAvadAshrayabhAvitvameva grAhyam.h | tatrApi visheSha eva saN^karaM vArayiShyatIti tu nirastam.h | kiJNcha pramANAnusAriNakSha vyavasthA natu svechChAnusAriNI | pramANaM tu bhedAbhedAvavagAhata iti vakShyate | nanu anityadravyAshritA ekatvAdayo.api guNAH kiM bhedavantasteShAmapi dravyakAryatayA taduttarakShaNabhAvitvAditi | maivam.h | ukttottaratvAt.h | ukttaM hyetat.h | upAdAnadravyaM guNavadupAdeyatayA pariNamata iti |
SUDHA_5.ACIHanyatra parameshvarAt.h | jaDe vastunIti yAvat.h | satyeva dhamirNi sAmastyenochChedavanto ye dharmAste ubhayarUpiNo bhinnAbhinnA ityarthaH | abhibhavavyAvR^ittyarthaM sAmastyetyukttam.h | yadvA sAmastye dravyasyAvikalatve nAshAbhAve.api ye uchChedina iti vyAkhyeyam.h | kiM svasadbhAvavelAyAmabhedino.asadbhAvavelAyAM bhedina ityevaM kAlabhedena bhedAbhedAvityata ukttam.h- bhAva iti || svasadbhAvadashAyAmevobhayarUpakA ityarthaH | vinaShyasyAsattvena bhedachintAnavakAshAt.h | prAgatyantAbhede vinAshAsambhavAchcha | kuto bhinnAbhinnA ityata Aha- ta eveti ||
SUDHA_5.ACIHtathA hi | sarvadikShvapi sambandhAditi yadaMshataH saMyoga ityukttaM tadayukttam.h | anavasthApatteH | ghaTasaMyogo hi ghaTAMshasaMyogapUrvakaH | so.api tadaMshasaMyogapUrvakaH | nacheyaM niraMshe paramparA vishrAmyatIti vAchyam.h | aMshaparamparAyA avishramasyApyaN^gIkR^itatvAt.h | ataH pUrvapUrvasaMyogAnutpattAvuttarottarAnutpattiprasaN^gAdaMshataH saMyoga iti niyamo nopapadyata iti | tadidamasaN^gatam.h | yadyapyaMshata eva saMyogo yadyapi chAMsheShvaMshaparamparAyA avishramastathA.apyaMshAMshinorabhede naivAMshasaMyoga eva hi yasmAdaMshinaH saMyogo.ato nAnavastheti | 
SUDHA_5.ACIHayamabhisandhiH | syAdiyamanavasthA yadi sarvatrAMshata eva saMyoga iti vadatAmasmAkamaMshinaH saMyogoM.ashasaMyogenaiva jAyata ityabhiprAyaH syAt.h | nachaivam.h | kintu yo yasya aMshinaH saMyogaH sa tadaMshe vartate | niraMshasya tu saMyogaH kva nAma vartatAm.h | ataH paramANvoH saMyoge sati tad.hvR^ittyarthamaMsho.aN^gIkaraNIya iti | na hyevaM sati kAchidanavasthA.asti | anavasthitakAryakAraNabhUtAsiddhasaMyogaparamparAshrayaNAbhAvAt.h | etAvattu bhavet.h | ghaTasaMyogaH syAt.h | pramANavirodhAchcha | ghaTasaMyogo ghaTavR^ittirapi ghaTasaMyogaH syAt.h | pramANavirodhAchcha | ghaTasaMyogo ghaTavR^ittistadguNatvAttadrUpavaditi | ghaTAMshavR^ittiH saMyogo na ghaTasaMyogaH tadanyavR^ittitvAt.h | paTasaMyogavaditi | etadapyanavakAsham.h | aMshAMshinorabhedasya sAdhitatvAt.h | atiprasaN^go hi tadA syAdyadi paTavadghaTAMsho.api ghaTAdatyantabhinnaH syAt.h | abhede tu kvAtiprasaN^gaH | anumAnasyApyAdyasya siddhasAdhanatA | aMshavR^ittereva ghaTavR^ittitvAt.h | aMshAvR^ittitve sati ghaTavR^ittitvasAdhane dR^iShyAntaH sAdhyavikalaH syAt.h | dvitIyastu hetuH svarUpAsiddho.anyathAsiddho veti | yadi ghaTasaMyogo ghaTAMshe vartate tarhi ghaTAMshasaMyogaH kva vartata iti chet.h | anena (eva) nyAyena tadaMshe so.api tadaMsha iti brUmaH | nachaivamanavasthA | sarve.apyaMshisaMyogAstattadaMshavR^ittaya ityatretarApekShAyA abhAvAt.h | 
SUDHA_5.ACIHevaM tarhi paramANuvR^ittirapi saMyogo ghaTasaMyogaH syAditi chet.h | ko netyAheti | aMshasaMyoga eva hyaMshinaH saMyogo.ato nAnavasthetyukttamanavasthAparihAraM vivR^iNoti- ekasminniti ||
SUDHA_5.ACIHavayavaparamparAyA avishramamabhyupagamyaikaikasminnavayavasaMyoge jAta evAnyo.avayavasaMyogo jAyata iti yadyaN^gIkurmastadaivAnavasthA syAt.h | saMyogaikye avayavisaMyogaH kriyAto jAtastadavayave vartate, avayavavR^itteH saMyogAdaparo.avayavinaH saMyogo nAstIti vAde tu, kva sA.anavastheti | 
SUDHA_5.ACIHastvanyasya saMyogo yathAtathA | prastute paramANau saMyogasyAMshavR^ittitvAbhAve nAtiprasaN^ga iti chenna | anvayavyatirekAbhyAM kAraNaparimANotkR^iShyasya kAryaparimANasya prachayAkhyAMshavR^ittisaMyogajatvAvadhAraNAtkAraNAbhAve cha kAryAbhAvaniyamAtparamANusaMyogasyAMshavR^ittitvAbhAve tatkArye dvayaNuke paramANuparimANAdutkR^iShyaparimANaM notpadyetetyasyaiva bAdhakasya sattvAt.h | nanvidamiShyApAdanam.h | paramANuto dvayaNuke parimANotkarShAbhAvAdityata Aha- paramANoriti || 
SUDHA_5.ACIHparamANuparimANAdaNodvaryaNukasya mahattA parimANotkarSho nAstIti vacho.adbhutaM svavyAhataM pramANaviruddhaM chetyarthaH | ayamADhyo.ayaM paramADhya itivadaNuparamANushabdAbhyAmeva parimANatAratamyAvagatestadabhAvavachanaM svavyAhataM bhavati | dvitantukaparimANavada(saMmR^idi)samuditAvayavajanyadravyaparimANatvena dvayaNukaparimANasya paramANuparimANAdutkarShasyAnumAnAvagatvAchcheti |

SUDHA_5.ACIHdvayaNukAnAM parimANotkarShApekShAM vinaiva saMkhyAmAtreNa tyaNuke sa parimANotkarSho jAyate | tathA paramANormahattvaM parimANotkarShaM vinA kevalasaMkhyayA dvayaNuke parimANotkaSharo jAyata ityetadvachaH kathaM ghaTate | mahaddIrghavadveti nirastatvAditi bhAvaH | chApishabdAvitaretarasamuchchaye | atra parimANamAtragrahaNe kartavye prathimeti mahattvamiti chokttirvisadR^ishaparimAratvasyAnapekShAhetoH nirAkaraNaM smArayitumiti | 
SUDHA_5.ACIHnanvevaM tarhi vyatiShakttatantuvyatirekeNa paTAbhAve paramANupuJNjavAdApattiriti | maivam.h | yathA hi guNAnAM dravyAbhede(.api) na dravyaM nirguNam.h | yathA cha pareShAM sAmAnyAdAvatirikttasattAbhAve(.api) nAsattvam.h | tathA vyatiShakttatantava eva paTastathA.api na paTAbhAvaH | kintu sati vyatiShakttAstantavaH paTashcha | sa cha tebhyo na bhidyate iti | kathametaditi chet.h | visheShashaktayaiveti brUmaH | 
SUDHA_5.ACIHnanvevaM tarhi saMyogAderapyekaikAshritatvaM na vakttavyam.h | ayAvaddravyabhAvitvena bhedAbhedAbhyAmevokttAkShepasamAdhAnAditi | satyam.h | tathA.api vastusthitiriyamukttetyadoShaH | api chAjasaMyoge nAyaM samAdhiH sambhavati | sa eva nAsti pramANAbhAvAditi chenna | paramANoH AkAshAdisaMyogAN^gIkArAt.h | so.api paramANukarmaja iti chenna | prAgasayogaprasaN^gAt.h | aMshabhedAnneti chenna | svAbhAvikasyAnabhyupagamAt.h | aupAdhikasya cha nirAkariShyamANatvAt.h | 
SUDHA_5.ACIHprAbhAkarAstvAhuH | sAdR^ishyaM tAvadekamanekAnugataM, tatra dharmatvahetovyarbhichAraH  nacha vAchyaM sAmAnyameva sAdR^ishyamataH pakShe vyabhichArachodaneyamanupapanneti | jAtisaN^karaprasaN^gAt.h | asti hi kayoshchidashvarAsabhavaktayoH sAdR^ishyaM, tatra yadi sAdR^ishyamashvatvAtparam.h tadA sarveShAmapyashvAnAM rAsabhasAdR^ishyaM syAt.h | yadi chAparaM tadA rAsabhavyakttAvapyashvatvaM syAt.h | evaM rAsabhatve.api vAchyam.h | na sAdR^ishyamashvarAsabhavR^itti brUmaH | kintu tadavayavR^itti | dravyaguNAvayavakarmavR^ittIni sAmAnyAdeva hi sAdR^ishyanAmanyabhyupagachChAmo.ato na jAiAtasaN^karadoSha iti chenna | gaurgavayena sadR^ishItyAdivyavahArANAmamukhyatvaprasaN^gAt.h | nacha sAmAnyaM pratiyoginirUpyam.h | tannirUpyaM cha sAdR^ishyamiti sphuTo.anayorbheda ityata Aha- etAdR^ishaM cheti ||
SUDHA_5.ACIHnanu ghaTAderAmadravyasyAgninA sambaddhasya, agnyabhighAtAnnodanAdvA tadArambhakeShu paramANuShu, karmANyutpadyante | tebhyo vibhAgAH, vibhAgebhyassaMyogavinAshAH | saMyogavinAshebhyaH kAryadravyaM vinashyati | tasminvichaShye paramANuShvagnisaMyogAdauShNyApekShAchChyAmAdInAM vinAshaH | punaranyasmAdagnisaMyogAdauShNyApekShAtpAkajA jAyante | tadanantaraM bhoginAmadR^iShyApekShAdAtmANusaMyogAdutpannapAkajeShvaNuShu karmotpattau teShAM parasparasaMyogAddvayaNukAdikrameNa kAryadravyamutpadyate | tatra cha kAraNaguNaprakrameNa rUpAdyutpattirbhavati | tatkathamAmaghaTashyAmatvAdInAmayAvad.hdravyabhAvitvamuchyate | 
SUDHA_5.ACIHnodanAdyutpattau karmotpattiH pramANam.h, karmasu vibhAgAH, teShu pUrvasaMyoganivR^ittiH, tatra kAryadravyavinAshaH, tatra cha pUrvarUpAdiparAvR^ittiH, tathA rUpAdyantarotpattiH sthUladravyotpattau pramANam.h, sA tadavayavaparamparAyAm.h, sA dvayaNuke, tadutpattiH paramANusaMyoge, sa cha tatkriyAyam.h, sA tadavayavaparamparAyAm.h, sA tadavayavaparamparAyAm.h, sA dvayaNuke, tadutpattiH paramANusaMyoge, sa cha tatkriyAyAm.h, sA.adR^iShyavadAtmasaMyoga iti chenna | paramANuShviva kAryadravyeShu pUrvarUpAdinivR^itterapUvarrUpAdyutpatterupapatteH | pArthivAvayavirUpAdayaH svAshrayavinAshAdeva vinashyanti avayavirUpAditvAt.h dagdhapaTarUpAdivat.h | kAraNaguNebhya evotpadyante tata eva tadvadeveti chenna | kvachitsatyAshraye.api rUpA(dInAM vi)divinAshe.agnisaMyogajatve cha virodhAbhAvAt.h | anyathA kAryadravyaM saMyogavinAshAdeva vinashyati kAryadravyatvAt.h dvayaNukavadityAdikamapi syAt.h | 
SUDHA_5.ACIHastvayaM gaurityAdivAkyaM vyAptiparam.h | tataH kimityata Aha- shakttiriti ||
SUDHA_5.ACIHtathA hi | sarvamapyanumAnaM na vastusvarUpamAtraparam.h | tasyAsiddhAvAshrayAsiddheH | siddhau cha siddhasAdhanatvAt.h | kintu kenachidupahitaM vA vishiShyaM vopalakShitaM veti vakttavyam.h | tachcha vishiShyAdikaM na visheShaNAditrayAdanyadeveti yukttam.h | anupalambhAdibAdhAt.h | trayAnanyatve.api na visheShaNamAtram.h | tasya anumAnAtprAk.h siddhatvAt.h | asiddhau chAprasiddhavisheShaNatvApatteH | agnerevAgnimachChabdArthatve matupo vaiyarthyApatteshcha | nApi dharmisvarUpamAtram.h | ukttadoShAt.h | parvato.agnimAnityetayerekArthatvApatteshcha | nacha sambandhamAtram.h | saMyogo hi kvachitsambandhaH syAt.h yathA.agniparvatayoH | kvachitsamavAyaH yathA rAsadrUpAnumAne | dvAvapi svarUpataH siddhAviti siddhasAdhanameva | saMyogamAtrasya siddhatve.apyagnyAdisaMyogaH sAdhya ityapi na vAchyam.h | tasyApi mahAnasAdau siddhatvAt.h | atha parvatAderagnyAdisaMyogaH sAdhyaH | atrApi vivekttavyam.h | kasyAtrAsiddhayA sAdhyatvamiti | anyasyAsambhavAt.h | ShaShThayarthasya samavAyasyeti vakttavyam.h | sa cha sarvatraika eva chetpunaH 
SUDHA_5.ACIHetadukttaM bhavati | nIlapaTasadbhAve.api pItapaTAbhAva ityatra hi yadi vishiShyaviShayau vidhiniShedhau, tadA bhinnaviShayatvena virodhAbhAvaH | nIlapItapaTayorbhinnatvAt.h | nachaivaM prakR^ite | bhedavisheShAbhAve.api bhedAntarAbhyupagamApatteH | tathA chaikatvokttirayukttaiva | nahi pArthivaparamANau rUpAdayo.agnisaMyogajA na tvApyaparAmANurUpAdaya iva svAbhAvikA ityetAvatA rUpAdirahito.asau bhavati | yadi cha visheShaNaviShayau tadA samavAye bhedo.astyeva | sa tu sambandhibhirupAdhibhiH kR^ito na tvakR^itrima ityukttaM syAt.h | tathAcha ghaTAdibhedena tulya iti rikttaivAbhedokttiH | upAdhInAM cha sarvadA.anapAyAnna bhedasyAgantukatvaM yukttamiti | 
SUDHA_6.ACIHyatsaMyogena hi yadvastUtpannaM tasminvidAraNe sati saMyoganAshAdvastunAshAnantaraM tadavasheSho bhavati | yathA tantusaMyogenotpanne ghaTe tantuvidAraNasaMyoganAshakrameNa vinaShye tantvavasheShaH | evaMcha yadi keShAJNchitparamAlpAnAM vastUnAM shUnyasaMyogAdutpattiH syAttadA vidAraNe sati saMyoganAshena kAryanAshe shUnyAvasheShaH syAt.h | nachaivaM prAmANikairiShyate | ato.asaN^gataM sarvashUnyatApAdanamiti | bhAvo janma |

SUDHA_6.ACIHtattadviShayatA ghaTAdiviShayatA, vidhIyate astitvenAN^gIkriyate | mA bhUttattadviShayatvamityata uktam.h- sArvaj~nArthamiti || upalakShaNaM chaitat.h | sarvakartR^itvAdyarthaM chetyapi draShyavyam.h | atrAnantavisheShA iti yathAgamasiddhoktiH | vastutastu yadi Ishvaraj~nAnAdi nirvisheShaM syAttadA tattadviShayatvaM na syAt.h | tadA cha tasya sArvaj~nAdikaM na syAt.h | sarvaviShayaj~nAnavAnhi sarvaj~no nAma | tathA sarvakAryotpattiviShayechChAprayatnavAnsarvakartA | sarvakAryavinAshaviShayechChAdimAMshcha sarvasaMhartA | aN^gIkR^itaM cha sArvaj~nAdi pareNa parameshvarasya | atastadarthaM j~nAnAdestattadviShayatayA bhAvyam.h | kathaM cha tathA sati nirvisheShatvamiti |

SUDHA_6.ACIHvaisheShikAdayo hi kAlavisheShe dvayaNukAdiprakrameNa mahAbhUtasR^iShyimabhyupagachChanti | tattadIyaprakriyAparyAlochanAyAM nopapadyate | kintu tatpakShe kAryaM sadA bhavet.h | yadA.abhilaShyate tataH prAgapi bhavet.h | kutaH | kAraNasAmagrIsampattinibandhano hi kAryotpatteH kAlaniyamaH | tatrAdisR^iShyau paramANavaH samavAyikAraNabhUtAstAvatsadA vidyante | nimittakAraNaM cheshvarechChA nityaiva | tathA kAlo di(kcha)k.h | yadyapyadR^iShyaM dharmAdharmasamAkhyAtaM na nityaM tathA.api pralaye.astItyaN^gIkriyata eva | vR^ittilAbhastadA nAstIti chenna | tasyApIshvarechChAdikAraNakasya tadbhAve.abhAvAnupapatteH | ata eva paramANusaMyogasyAsamavAyikAraNasyAbhAvAnna sadA sR^i(sadAdisR^i)(mahadAdisR^i)Shyiriti nirastam.h | saMyogAnutpAdasyApyanupapatteH | tadasamavAyikAraNakarmAbhAvAditi chenna | tadanutpAdasyApyayogAt.h | nachAto.anyadvayaNukAdeH kAraNamasti | yadvaikalyAdabhilaShitasamayAtprAk.h kAryAbhAvo bhavet.h | satyAM chAbhimatasAmagyrAM kAryAnudaye pashchAdapi notpadyeta | niyAmakAbhAvAditi | sadAtvaM sadAtatvanam.h | bhAvAt.h pralaye.apIti sheShaH | evashabdasya sadaiveti sambandhaH | kAryaM bhavediti chAbhyupagamyoktam.h | vastutastu tatpakShe kadA.api dvayaNukAdyutpattirna sambhavati | vinAshakAraNasyeshvarechChAdeH sadAtanatvena satpratipakShatvAt.h | kAryotpattisahakR^itameveshvarechChAdikaM vinAshakAraNamityaN^gIkAre.apyutpattyanantarameva vinAshaH prasajyeteti | ata eva sR^iShyayAdIti vakShyati | 
SUDHA_6.ACIHnanu kAlavisheShANAM parameshvarAjjanma kutaH pramANAtsiddhamityata Aha- sarva iti ||

SUDHA_6.ACIHparamANoriti jAtyapekShamekavachanam.h | pArthivAdInAM chaturvidhAnAM paramANUnAM nityatAmupayAnti vaisheShikAdayaH | tadanupapannam.h | pAthirvAH pAthasIyAstaijasAshcha paramANavo.anityA rUpavattvAtpaTavat.h | yadvA chaturvidhA apyanityAH sparshavattvAtpaTavat.h | evaM pArthitavA ApyAshchAnityA rasavattvAtpaTavat.h | pArthivA anityA gandhavattvAttadvadevetyAdyanumAnaviruddhatvAt.h | nacha sAvayavatvamupAdhiH | guNAdau sAdhyAvyApteH | nacha dravyatvAvachChinne sAdhye.asyopAdhitvam.h | yadrUpAdimattatsAvayavamiti sAdhanavyApakatvAt.h | nacha dharmigrAhakavirodhaH | sAkShiNaiva paramANusiddheruktatvAt.h | anityatve cha paramANUnAM na mUlakAraNatvasiddhiH | yadi cha rUpAdimanto.api paramANavo nAnityAstadA ghaTAdayo.apyanityA na syuravisheShAt.h | tathA.a(cha)pi na paramANUnAM mUlakAraNatvam.h | nacheshvare hetUnAM vyabhichAraH | bhautikatvena visheShaNAt.h | tathAcha vakShyati | "bhautikaM tveva rUpAdi vyAptaM nAshena no mate' | iti |

SUDHA_6.ACIHkAlakarmaNI cha te nimitte cha tataH | utpattikAle AdisR^iShyau | anyadA tu nimittAntaramastIti bhAvaH | yuktAnAM sannikR^iShyatayotpannAnAmaNUnAM samudAyamiti sambandhaH | karmAdivashAdeva tathA tathA sannikR^iShyAH paramANavo jAyante | yatA yathA goghaTAdivichitrAkArAvabhAsaH syAt.h | tatra kimIshvareNa | kiM vA.avayavinA | siddhAntinA.api hi karmAdikaM nimittamaN^gIkartavyam.h | saMyogashchAvayavyutpAdAnuguNaH | tAvataiva sarvamupapadyata itrata |

SUDHA_6.ACIHsamudAyasya samuditAnekeShAM chetaretarApekShotpattikatvenetyarthaH | samudAyAnu(tpattau) chANUnAM mahAneka iti pratyakShabuddhigocharatA.ayogAdavashyamaN^gIkaraNIyo.avayavIti | kiJNchAyaM samudAyaH kiM paramANUnAM saMyogaH kiMvA.anekatvasaN^khayA | uta dravyAntaram.h | nAdyadvitIyau | anaN^gIkArAt.h | aN^gIkAre.apyatIndriyAshritayostayoraindriyakatvAnupapattiH | tR^itIye sa evAvayavI | sAMvR^ito.asAviti chet.h | tarhi punarmahAnityAdipramAnupapattistadavasthaiva | bhrAntiriyamiti chet.h(na) | bhrAnterabhrAntipUrvakatvena kvachinmahattvAdevarAstavattvaprasaN^gAt.h | anAdivAsanAvashAdAnAdireveyaM bhrAntiriti chenna | nIlAdij~nAnasyApi tathAtvaprasaN^gAt.h | 
SUDHA_6.ACIHbhavedidamanyonyAshrayatvaM yadyayaM samudAyaH kAdAchitkaH syAt.h | nachaivam.h | sadAtanaM tvimamabhyupagachChAmaH | evaM tarhi sR^iShyipralayavyavasthA na syAditi chenna | yatastasya samudAyasya sadAtanatve.api puMsaH samudAyatvavedanaM syAt.h | kadAchiditi sheShaH | tatastadapekShayA sR^iShyayAdivvayasthopapadyata iti bhAvaH | samudAyasya sadAtanatve tadvedanamapi kutaH kAdAchitkamityata uktam.h- tachcheti || tatsamudAyatvavedanaM paramANusAmIpyahetukam.h | nacha sAmIpyaM sadA.astIti vedanasya kAdAchitkatvamiti | samudAyatvavedanasya sAmIpyahetukatA kuta ityata (uktaM) Aha- anyonyeti || anyonyaparamANuj~nAnApekShayA hi tadbhavati | nachAnyonyaj~nAnaM sAmIpyena vinA bhavatIti |
SUDHA_6.ACIHetaduktaM bhavati | aneke paramANava eva samudAyaH | tadanekatvaM cha samudAyatvam.h | tanmiliteShviva viraleShvapi vidyate | kintu na sadA samudAyatvavedanaM bhavati | itaraparamANusahitetaraparamANusahitetaraparamANuj~nAne sati hi samudAyatvaj~nAnaM bhavati | apekShAbuddheranekatvavyaJNjakatvAt.h | nachetaretaraparamANuj~nAne sati hi samudAyatvaj~nAnaM bhavati | apekShAbuddheranekatvavyaJNjakatvAt.h | nachetaretaraparamANuj~nAne sati hi samudAyatvaj~nAnaM bhavati | ma(thu)dhurApATalIputrasthitayorvR^ikShayoritaretarapratyayo dR^iShyaH | kiJNchAdhipatisahakAyarAlambanasamanantarapratyayAshchatvAro hi j~nAnahetavaH | adhipatirindriyam.h | nacha viralAnAM paramANUnAmindriyAlambanaviralaparamANubhyastadAlambanatayA tathAtathA sannikR^iShyAH paramANavo jAyante | anadhipatIndriyebhyashchAdhipatIndriyANi | athedAnIM samanantarapratyayabalAdeko mahAniti j~nAnamutpadyate | tena nAnyonyAshrayatvam.h | nApi sR^iShyayAdyanupapattiriti |

SUDHA_6.ACIHidamatra vaktavyam.h | sadvAdimatAnusaraNasamaye.asattvAdibhaN^gIraN^gIkaroShi (vA) na veti | evamasadvAdicharaNasharaNapraveshavelAyAM sattvAdiprakArAnUrIkaroShi vA na veti | evamanyeShvapi pakSheShu vikalpaH | yadyAdyastadA.asau achaladarshanaH sadA sakalapakShAN^gIkAravAn.h tairdoShairakhilai(tairakhilairdoShai)rlipyate | tathAhi | sadvAdino hi na kevalaM sattve pramANaM tadanaN^gIkAre cha dUShaNaM cha vyutpAdya nivR^ittAH | kintvasattvAdipakSheShu doShAnapi vyutpAditavantaH | evamasadvAdino.api nAsattve pramANaM tadanabhyupagame bAdhakaM chAbhidhAyaivoparatA, kinnAma sattvAdipakSheShu doShAnapi upapAditavantaH | evamanye.api | tathAcha sakalapakShakakShIkAre (tu) tattadvAdyuktapakShAntaradoShalepaH kathaM na syAt.h | atha manyase | na te doShAH kintvAbhAsAH | te cha nAnekAntavAdaM bAdhanta iti | tadA kathaM tAni pramANAni | anaN^gIkAre doShAshcha nAbhAsAH | (ye nAnuma)yenAnusaraNIyAH | tasamttattadvAdivyutpAditapramANAdyanusAreNa saptabhaN^gIraN^gIkurvANena taduktavipakShadoShAnusAreNa tatparityAgo.api kAryaH syAt.h | tathA chAN^gIkAraparityAgAbhyAmubhayata AkR^iShyo.ayaM kaShyAM dashAmAviShyaH syAt.h | nanvekAnto dvedhA | kramAkramabhedAt.h | tatra kramAnekAnte tAvannAN^gIkAraparityAgau viruddhau | akramAnekAnte.api yena rUpeNa nityatvaM tenaivAnityatvamityAdyanaN^gIkArAnna virodhaH | tathAcha saptabhaN^gayaN^gIkAriNA mayA tAni pramANAni dUShaNAni cha vyavasthApitAni bhavantIti noktadoShaH | maivam.h | tattatpramANAdInAM vyavasthAnarhatvAt.h | na khalu tatta(tpramANavA)dvAdibhistAni tAni pramANAdIni sAvakAshAnyupanyastAni | tasmAtsarveShvapi (vAdiShu) vAdeShu paramAstikasya kathitaiva gatiH | api chaivamapi saptabhaN^gayaN^gIkAro nirmUla eva | na hyevaMvAdino vAdinaH prasiddhAH | sambhAvanayA tadaN^gIkAre cha na saptatvapariniShThA | sambhAvanAvakA(ko)shasya niHsImatvAt.h | kiJNcha sarvAN^gIkArapakShe syAdasti cha nAsti cheti pakShAtsyAdasti syAnnAstIti pakShadvayaM na bhidyate | 
SUDHA_6.ACIHasheShamAviruddhaM sadA sarvaprakAratvaM vadato dR^iShyahAniH syAt.h | nirmAna cha sadA sarvaprakAraM vadato amagraho aprAmANikasvIkAraH syAt.h | vyAhataM sadA sarvaprakAraM vadataH svavyAhatatvaM syAditi yojanA | dR^iShyahAnAdyanuShaN^gidoShAntarasaN^grahArthamityAdyA ityuktam.h | hishabdaH sarvatra prasaN^gahetusUchanArthaH | ayamarthaH | yadi pramANaviruddhamapi sarvaprakAratvaM vishvasya svIkriyate tadA dahanashaityaM vA gavAlambhanAderdharmasAdhanatvAdikaM vA(chA).aN^gIkAryaM syAt.h | pramANavirodhena pratipakShanirAkaraNaM cha na syAt.h | kintu pratyabhij~nAdiviruddhamapi kShaNikatvAdikamaN^gIkartavyaM syAt.h | avisheShAt.h | yadi chAprAmANikamapi sarvaprakAratvamurarIkriyate tadA kharaviShANAdikaM vA gomAMsAdibhakShaNasya dharmasAdhanatvaM chorarIkaraNIyaM syAt.h | pramANAbhAvena paramatanirAso.api na kAryaH syAt.h | tada(pya)bhyupagamanIyameva bhavedavisheShAt.h | tathAcha dUShyopAdeyahInasya shAstranirmANamapi na syAt.h | yadi cha vyAhatamapi sarvaprakAratvamaN^gIkuryAt.h tadA mAturapi vandhyatvaM, jinopadeshasya pramANatayA.abhyupagatasyApyaprAmANyaM, baddhasyApi muktatvaM, muktasyApi baddhatvaM, siddhasyApi rAgitvaM, shvapachasyApi siddhatvamityAdisarvamapyaN^gI(kuryAt.h)kAryaM syAt.h | anyathA.anekAntabhaN^gaprasaN^gAt.h | evaMcha na shAstrapraNayanaprayAsaH kAryaH | mattonmattAdibhirevAsya kR^itatvAditi |
SUDHA_6.ACIHivashabdo.adhyAhAryaH | pudgalasya dehasyeveti | yadvA pudgalashabdo jarajjainairAtmavAchitvena svIkR^ita ityatrAtmavAchI | (yadvA) yadi vA svamatenAyamAtmani prayuktaH | yathA.a.ahuH | "pudgalo nirayayaM giran.h' iti | nanvavasthAparyAyarUpeNA(pyA)tmano.apyanityatvamaN^gIkriyata eva | tatkathamanityatvApAdanamityato vA pudgalasya dehasyevetyuktam.h | yathA dehasya dehAkAranAmaparityAgena bhasmIbhAvalakShaNAnityatvaM tathAvidhamAtamno.apyApAdyata iti | nanu anyathAbhAvasyaivaM vidhAnityatvena vyAptirnAsti paramANvAdau vyabhichArAt.h | tatkathamApAdanam.h | maivam.h | parimANavyatyayalakShaNasyAnyathAbhAvasyaivaMvidhAnityatvavyAptatvena dehAdau dR^iShyatayA tadvato.apyAtmanastathAvidhAnityatvasya nivArayitumashakyatvAt.h | tadidamuktam.h- anivAritamiti ||

SUDHA_6.ACIH|| OM sandhye sR^iShyirAha hi OM || yoneH sharIramityetadavasAnaiH sUtrairjIvasya janmAvagatam.h | jAtasya cha svapanAdyavasthAsambandhaH prasiddhaH | tatra svapnAvasthApravartakatvalakShaNo mahimAbhagavato.atrAdhikaraNe nirNIyate | tathAhi | svapno nAmArthaj~nAnAtmakaH | tatra tAvatsvApnArthAnAM karituragAdInAM parameshvarAyattatA nopapadyate | asatyatvAt.h | na tAvadime.anAdinityAH | svapnAvasthAtaH prAgUrdhvaM chopalabdhiprasaN^gAt.h | nahi vidyamAnA apyupalabdhisAdhaneShu chakShurAdiShvanuparateShu nopalabhyante, upalabhyante chopapatteriti sambhavati | nachAnyatra gatAH | anyairapyanupalambhAt.h | madyamaparimANashchaite dR^ishyante | nacha tathAvidhamanAdinityaM kimapi dR^iShyam.h | nApyutpattinAshavantaH | tathAtve.api prAgUrdhvamupalambhaprasakteH | nacha vAchyaM vidyudAdivattadaivotpattirvinAshashcheti | itthambhAve pramANAbhAvAt.h | prAD.hmR^idAdInAmUrdhvaM kapAlAdInAM chopalambhApatteshcha | nachaiteShAM (tAtkAlika)tatkAlInajanmanyupAdAnaM nimittaM cha pashyAmaH | kartA cha na tAvajjIvAtmA | draShyurnivyarApAratvAt.h | aparasya chAdarshanAt.h | nApIshvaraH | pramANAbhAvAt.h | bhrAntitvaM chaiteShAm.h, "svApnamAyAsarUpaH' iti "svApnamanoratho yathA' ityAdishrutismR^itibhyAmAvedyate | shiShyamapavyAkhyAnAnuvAde vakShyAmaH | tadevaM na svApnAnAmarthAnAmIshvarAdhInatvam.h | nApi tajj~nAnasya | tasyApi nimittAbhAvenAparamArthatvAt.h | natAvachchakShurAdInAM ta(tra nimi)nnimittatvam.h | teShAmuparatatvAt.h | nApi manasaH | rUpAdimatyarthe sAmarthyAbhAvAt.h (svAtantAbhAvAt.h) | ata eva na sAkShiNaH | sa indriyApravR^ittau liN^gashabdayorapi nAvakAshaH | aparokShAkAraM chedamavabhAsate | ato.arthaj~nAnarUpA svApnAvasthA neshvarAdhIneti prApte tatpratividhAnAyopodghAtamAha- vAsanA iti ||

SUDHA_6.ACIHevaM prApte pratyAha- mAyAmAtraM tu kAtsnaryenAnabhivyaktasvarUpatvAt.h | tushabdaH pakShaM vyAvartayati | mAyetyanAdiranirvAchyA.avidyochyate | mAyaiva sandhye sR^iShyirna paramArthagandho.apyasti | kutaH | mAyetyanAdiranirvAchy.avidyochyate | mAyaiva sandhye sR^iShyirna paramArthagandho.apyasti | kutaH | kAtsnaryenAnabhivyaktasvarUpatvAt.h | deshakAlanimittasampattirabAdhashcha kAtsnaryaM tenAbhivyaktasvarUpatvAbhAvAt.h |
SUDHA_6.ACIHsUchakashcha hi shruterAchakShate cha tadvidaH | mAyAmAtratvAttarhi na kashchitsvapne paramArthagandha iti netyuchyate | sUchakashcha hi svapno bhavati bhaviShyatoH sAdhvasAdhunoH | kutaH | yadA karmasvityAdishruteH | AchakShate cha svapnAdhyAyavidaH | tatra bhavatu sUchyamAnasya satyatvam.h | sUchakasya tu vaitathyameveti bhAvaH | 
SUDHA_6.ACIHparAbhidhyAnAttu tirohitaM tato hyasya bandhaviparyayau | nanyagneraMshasya viShphuliN^gasya yathA dahanaprakAshanashaktI bhavatastatheshvarAMshasya jIvasyApi j~nAnaishvaryashaktibhyAM bhAvyam.h | tatashcha sAN^kalpikI sR^iShyiH syAdityasyedamuttaram.h | satyamastyeveshvarasAdharmyaM jIvasya kintu tirohitam.h | tattu parameshvarAbhidhyAnAdevAvirbhavati | kutaH | tato hIshvarAddhetorasya jIvasya bandhamokShau bhavataH | dehayogAdvA so.api | kasmAjjIvasya j~nAnaishvaryatiraskAro bhavati | viShphuliN^gavadatiraskAro hi yukta ityatredamuttaram.h | so.api tiraskAro jIvasya dehayogAt.h | avidyApratyupasthApitanAmarUpakR^itadehendriyamanobuddhiviShayavedanAdyupAdhiyogAttadavivekabhramakR^ito bhavati | yathA.araNiyogAdagneH | kimanayA kalpanayA | anya evAstu jIvaH parameshvarAdityetadvAshabdena | vyavachChinatti | maivam.h | tattvamasyAdishrutivirodhAditi |

SUDHA_7.ACIHkiJNcha viditatattvo.api yadA paraparIkShArthaM (dyarthe) tatra pramANaM pR^ichChati | tadA prayuktamanumAnamamAnaM syAt.h | sandehAbhAvAt.h | tasmAtsandigdhasAdhyaH pakSha ityAdyAH prAchAM vAchaH sambhAvanAbhiprAyAH | paramArthatastvanumitiviShaya eva pakShaH | ataH sandehAbhAve pakShatvAnupapattyabhAvAnnAprasiddhasAdhane pakShadharmatvAsiddhirUpo doSha iti |

SUDHA_7.ACIHdR^iShyAntadoShAMshcha kechidaShyAvAchakShate | sAdhyavaikalyaM sAdhanavaikalyamubhayavaikalyamAshrayahInatvamiti chatvAraH sAdharmyadR^iShyAntadoShAH | sAdhyAvyAvR^ittiH sAdhanAvyAvR^ittirubhayAvyAvR^ittirAshrayahInatvamiti chatvAro vaidhamyardR^iShyAntadoShA iti | tannetyAha- sAdhyeti || siddhe satyArambho niyamArthaH | sAdhyasAdhanavaikalyameva dR^iShyAntasya dUShaNaM nAparamityarthaH | tathAhi | ubhayavaikalyaM tAvatpR^ithaN^.h na vAchyam.h | ekaikavaikalyenaiva dR^iShyAntasya duShyatve samuditakalpanAvaiyarthyAt.h | anyathaikaikavaikalyasya dUShaNatvAN^gIkArabhaN^gAt.h | sambhavamAtreNa pR^ithagvachane.anaikAntikakAlatItatvaM nAma hetvAbhAsAntaraM vAchyaM syAt.h | AshrayahInatvaM chAshrayasiddhisamAnam.h | vaidharmyadR^iShyAnto nAma nAstyeveti prAgeva prapaJNchitamiti |

SUDHA_7.ACIHtadadhInatvaM paramAtmAdhInatvam.h | asheShato.asheSheShu vyApAreShu | sandhye sR^iShyirAha hItyAdau | sadR^ishatvaM cha paramAtmanA, yaduktaM puMstvAdivadityAdau kiM tatsadR^ishatvam.h, chittvamAtram.h | na chAparaM svAtantAdikaM, yena hetorviruddhatA syAditi bhAvaH |

SUDHA_7.ACIH|| OM paramataH setUnmAnasambandhabhedavyapadeshebhyaH OM || parameshvarasyAnandAdayo guNAH kiM laukikAnandAdisalakShaNAH kiM vA tadvilakShaNAH | Adye na tatra bahumAnaH sambhavati | na dvitIyaH | prakArapramANAbhAvAt.h | vimatA laukikasalakShaNA AnandAdishabdavAchyatvAditi bAdhakasadbhAvAchcha | anyathA tatrAnandAdishabdapravR^ittirna syAt.h | vyutpattyabhAvAt.h | atIndriyatvena tatropadeshA(dyupAyAdya)bhAve sAdR^ishyAnumAnasyaivAnusaraNIyatvAt.h | tasya chAsiddhatvAt.h | tatashcha vedavedyatvaM na syAdityasya samAdhAnArthamidamArabhyate | tatrAshaN^kitasakaladoShaparihAro na sphuTaH pratIyata ityato vyAchaShye- te cheti ||
SUDHA_7.ACIHAnukUlyaM nirupAdhipriyatvamAnandasya | bodhAtmakatvaM j~nAnasyetyAdi | aparamalpatvAsthiratvAdi | AnukUlyAdeH pravR^ittinimittasya sattvAttadAshrayeNa vyutpatterapi sambhavAdAnandAdishabdapravR^ittyupapattAvanumAnamaprayojakamityuktaM bhavati | nanu vilakShaNeShvAnandAdiShu vilakShaNA eva shabdAH kuto na prayujyante | tathA sati tatra buddhipraveshAbhAvaprasaN^gAt.h | alpatvAdisAdR^ishyaM kuto netyata Aha- pUrNatvAdIti ||

SUDHA_7.ACIHsAmyApattirityapi na vAchyam.h | yataH phaladAne parameshvaraH kartR^itvena karma tu kAraNatvena puNyena puNyamityAdau vyapadishyate | karaNaM cha kartR^iprayojyamiti prasiddhameveti | tatredamAshaN^kayate | tathA.api karmApekShasyeshvarasya phaladAne.anupacharitaM svAtantyaM na siddhayati | tatashcha na tasminbahumAnAtishaya iti | etatparihAratvena pUrvapadaM vyAkhyAti- sa eveti ||

SUDHA_8.ACIHtat.h tasmAtpUrvasUtragatasyAtmashabdasya paramAtmavAchitvAnna pratIka iti pratij~nAvAkyasya pratIkaviShayatvena viShNudR^iShTiH kartavyA na bhavedityevArthaH | idamukttaM bhavati | na pratIka ityatra tAvadAtmetItyanuvartanIyaM pUrvasUtrAt.h | anyathA pratij~nAvAkyasyAparipUrNatvAt.h | pUrvasUtre chAtmashabdo viShNuviShaya iti samarthitam.h | tathAcha pratIkaviShayAyA viShNudR^iShyerevAyaM pratiShedho vyAkhyeyaH | na pratIkeShu jIvamatiM badhnIyAditi tu pratij~nAvyAkhyAne prakR^itaparityAgo.aprakR^itasvIkArashcha prasajyeyAtAmiti |
